<s> Extracts from Adam's Diary Eve's Diary THE $30,000 BEQUEST CHAPTER I Lakeside was a pleasant little town of five or six thousand inhabitants, and a rather pretty one, too, as towns go in the Far West </s>
<s> It had church accommodations for thirty-five thousand, which is the way of the Far West and the South, where everybody is religious, and where each of the Protestant sects is represented and has a plant of its own </s>
<s> Rank was unknown in Lakeside--unconfessed, anyway; everybody knew everybody and his dog, and a sociable friendliness was the prevailing atmosphere </s>
<s> Saladin Foster was book-keeper in the principal store, and the only high-salaried man of his profession in Lakeside </s>
<s> He was thirty-five years old, now; he had served that store for fourteen years; he had begun in his marriage-week at four hundred dollars a year, and had climbed steadily up, a hundred dollars a year, for four years; from that time forth his wage had remained eight hundred--a handsome figure indeed, and everybody conceded that he was worth it </s>
<s> His wife, Electra, was a capable helpmeet, although--like himself--a dreamer of dreams and a private dabbler in romance </s>
<s> The first thing she did, after her marriage--child as she was, aged only nineteen--was to buy an acre of ground on the edge of the town, and pay down the cash for it--twenty-five dollars, all her fortune </s>
<s> Saladin had less, by fifteen </s>
<s> She instituted a vegetable garden there, got it farmed on shares by the nearest neighbor, and made it pay her a hundred per cent </s>
<s> a year </s>
<s> Out of Saladin's first year's wage she put thirty dollars in the savings-bank, sixty out of his second, a hundred out of his third, a hundred and fifty out of his fourth </s>
<s> His wage went to eight hundred a year, then, and meantime two children had arrived and increased the expenses, but she banked two hundred a year from the salary, nevertheless, thenceforth </s>
<s> When she had been married seven years she built and furnished a pretty and comfortable two-thousand-dollar house in the midst of her garden-acre, paid half of the money down and moved her family in </s>
<s> Seven years later she was out of debt and had several hundred dollars out earning its living </s>
<s> Earning it by the rise in landed estate; for she had long ago bought another acre or two and sold the most of it at a profit to pleasant people who were willing to build, and would be good neighbors and furnish a general comradeship for herself and her growing family </s>
<s> She had an independent income from safe investments of about a hundred dollars a year; her children were growing in years and grace; and she was a pleased and happy woman </s>
<s> Happy in her husband, happy in her children, and the husband and the children were happy in her </s>
<s> It is at this point that this history begins </s>
<s> The youngest girl, Clytemnestra--called Clytie for short--was eleven; her sister, Gwendolen--called Gwen for short--was thirteen; nice girls, and comely </s>
<s> The names betray the latent romance-tinge in the parental blood, the parents' names indicate that the tinge was an inheritance </s>
<s> It was an affectionate family, hence all four of its members had pet names, Saladin's was a curious and unsexing one--Sally; and so was Electra's--Aleck </s>
<s> All day long Sally was a good and diligent book-keeper and salesman; all day long Aleck was a good and faithful mother and housewife, and thoughtful and calculating business woman; but in the cozy living-room at night they put the plodding world away, and lived in another and a fairer, reading romances to each other, dreaming dreams, comrading with kings and princes and stately lords and ladies in the flash and stir and splendor of noble palaces and grim and ancient castles </s>
<s> CHAPTER II Now came great news </s>
<s> Stunning news--joyous news, in fact </s>
<s> It came from a neighboring state, where the family's only surviving relative lived </s>
<s> It was Sally's relative--a sort of vague and indefinite uncle or second or third cousin by the name of Tilbury Foster, seventy and a bachelor, reputed well off and corresponding sour and crusty </s>
<s> Sally had tried to make up to him once, by letter, in a bygone time, and had not made that mistake again </s>
<s> Tilbury now wrote to Sally, saying he should shortly die, and should leave him thirty thousand dollars, cash; not for love, but because money had given him most of his troubles and exasperations, and he wished to place it where there was good hope that it would continue its malignant work </s>
<s> The bequest would be found in his will, and would be paid over </s>
<s> PROVIDED, that Sally should be able to prove to the executors that he had TAKEN NO NOTICE OF THE GIFT BY SPOKEN WORD OR BY LETTER, HAD MADE NO INQUIRIES CONCERNING THE MORIBUND'S PROGRESS TOWARD THE EVERLASTING TROPICS, AND HAD NOT ATTENDED THE FUNERAL </s>
<s> As soon as Aleck had partially recovered from the tremendous emotions created by the letter, she sent to the relative's habitat and subscribed for the local paper </s>
<s> Man and wife entered into a solemn compact, now, to never mention the great news to any one while the relative lived, lest some ignorant person carry the fact to the death-bed and distort it and make it appear that they were disobediently thankful for the bequest, and just the same as confessing it and publishing it, right in the face of the prohibition </s>
<s> For the rest of the day Sally made havoc and confusion with his books, and Aleck could not keep her mind on her affairs, not even take up a flower-pot or book or a stick of wood without forgetting what she had intended to do with it </s>
<s> For both were dreaming </s>
<s> "Thir-ty thousand dollars" </s>
<s> All day long the music of those inspiring words sang through those people's heads </s>
<s> From his marriage-day forth, Aleck's grip had been upon the purse, and Sally had seldom known what it was to be privileged to squander a dime on non-necessities </s>
<s> "Thir-ty thousand dollars" </s>
<s> the song went on and on </s>
<s> A vast sum, an unthinkable sum </s>
<s> All day long Aleck was absorbed in planning how to invest it, Sally in planning how to spend it </s>
<s> There was no romance-reading that night </s>
<s> The children took themselves away early, for their parents were silent, distraught, and strangely unentertaining </s>
<s> The good-night kisses might as well have been impressed upon vacancy, for all the response they got; the parents were not aware of the kisses, and the children had been gone an hour before their absence was noticed </s>
<s> Two pencils had been busy during that hour--note-making; in the way of plans </s>
<s> It was Sally who broke the stillness at last </s>

<s> Don't they pay half-yearly" </s>

<s> "For big returns" </s>
<s> "Big </s>

<s> But Aleck went down and put it out </s>

<s> CHAPTER III The little newspaper which Aleck had subscribed for was a Thursday sheet; it would make the trip of five hundred miles from Tilbury's village and arrive on Saturday </s>
<s> Tilbury's letter had started on Friday, more than a day too late for the benefactor to die and get into that week's issue, but in plenty of time to make connection for the next output </s>
<s> Thus the Fosters had to wait almost a complete week to find out whether anything of a satisfactory nature had happened to him or not </s>
<s> It was a long, long week, and the strain was a heavy one </s>
<s> The pair could hardly have borne it if their minds had not had the relief of wholesome diversion </s>
<s> We have seen that they had that </s>
<s> The woman was piling up fortunes right along, the man was spending them--spending all his wife would give him a chance at, at any rate </s>
<s> At last the Saturday came, and the WEEKLY SAGAMORE arrived </s>
<s> Mrs Eversly Bennett was present </s>
<s> She was the Presbyterian parson's wife, and was working the Fosters for a charity </s>
<s> Talk now died a sudden death--on the Foster side </s>
<s> Mrs Bennett presently discovered that her hosts were not hearing a word she was saying; so she got up, wondering and indignant, and went away </s>
<s> The moment she was out of the house, Aleck eagerly tore the wrapper from the paper, and her eyes and Sally's swept the columns for the death-notices </s>
<s> Disappointment </s>
<s> Tilbury was not anywhere mentioned </s>
<s> Aleck was a Christian from the cradle, and duty and the force of habit required her to go through the motions </s>
<s> She pulled herself together and said, with a pious two-per-cent </s>
<s> trade joyousness: "Let us be humbly thankful that he has been spared; and--" "Damn his treacherous hide, I wish--" "Sally </s>
<s> For shame" </s>
<s> "I don't care" </s>
<s> retorted the angry man </s>
<s> "It's the way YOU feel, and if you weren't so immorally pious you'd be honest and say so" </s>
<s> Aleck said, with wounded dignity: "I do not see how you can say such unkind and unjust things </s>
<s> There is no such thing as immoral piety" </s>
<s> Sally felt a pang, but tried to conceal it under a shuffling attempt to save his case by changing the form of it--as if changing the form while retaining the juice could deceive the expert he was trying to placate </s>
<s> He said: "I didn't mean so bad as that, Aleck; I didn't really mean immoral piety, I only meant--meant--well, conventional piety, you know; er--shop piety; the--the--why, YOU know what I mean </s>
<s> Aleck--the--well, where you put up that plated article and play it for solid, you know, without intending anything improper, but just out of trade habit, ancient policy, petrified custom, loyalty to--to--hang it, I can't find the right words, but YOU know what I mean, Aleck, and that there isn't any harm in it </s>
<s> I'll try again </s>
<s> You see, it's this way </s>
<s> If a person--" "You have said quite enough," said Aleck, coldly; "let the subject be dropped" </s>
<s> "I'M willing," fervently responded Sally, wiping the sweat from his forehead and looking the thankfulness he had no words for </s>
<s> Then, musingly, he apologized to himself </s>
<s> "I certainly held threes--I KNOW it--but I drew and didn't fill </s>
<s> That's where I'm so often weak in the game </s>
<s> If I had stood pat--but I didn't </s>
<s> I never do </s>
<s> I don't know enough" </s>
<s> Confessedly defeated, he was properly tame now and subdued </s>
<s> Aleck forgave him with her eyes </s>
<s> The grand interest, the supreme interest, came instantly to the front again; nothing could keep it in the background many minutes on a stretch </s>
<s> The couple took up the puzzle of the absence of Tilbury's death-notice </s>
<s> They discussed it every which way, more or less hopefully, but they had to finish where they began, and concede that the only really sane explanation of the absence of the notice must be--and without doubt was--that Tilbury was not dead </s>
<s> There was something sad about it, something even a little unfair, maybe, but there it was, and had to be put up with </s>
<s> They were agreed as to that </s>
<s> To Sally it seemed a strangely inscrutable dispensation; more inscrutable than usual, he thought; one of the most unnecessary inscrutable he could call to mind, in fact--and said so, with some feeling; but if he was hoping to draw Aleck he failed; she reserved her opinion, if she had one; she had not the habit of taking injudicious risks in any market, worldly or other </s>
<s> The pair must wait for next week's paper--Tilbury had evidently postponed </s>
<s> That was their thought and their decision </s>
<s> So they put the subject away and went about their affairs again with as good heart as they could </s>
<s> Now, if they had but known it, they had been wronging Tilbury all the time </s>
<s> Tilbury had kept faith, kept it to the letter; he was dead, he had died to schedule </s>
<s> He was dead more than four days now and used to it; entirely dead, perfectly dead, as dead as any other new person in the cemetery; dead in abundant time to get into that week's SAGAMORE, too, and only shut out by an accident; an accident which could not happen to a metropolitan journal, but which happens easily to a poor little village rag like the SAGAMORE </s>
<s> On this occasion, just as the editorial page was being locked up, a gratis quart of strawberry ice-water arrived from Hostetter's Ladies and Gents Ice-Cream Parlors, and the stickful of rather chilly regret over Tilbury's translation got crowded out to make room for the editor's frantic gratitude </s>
<s> On its way to the standing-galley Tilbury's notice got pied </s>
<s> Otherwise it would have gone into some future edition, for WEEKLY SAGAMORES do not waste "live" matter, and in their galleys "live" matter is immortal, unless a pi accident intervenes </s>
<s> But a thing that gets pied is dead, and for such there is no resurrection; its chance of seeing print is gone, forever and ever </s>
<s> And so, let Tilbury like it or not, let him rave in his grave to his fill, no matter--no mention of his death would ever see the light in the WEEKLY SAGAMORE </s>
<s> CHAPTER IV Five weeks drifted tediously along </s>
<s> The SAGAMORE arrived regularly on the Saturdays, but never once contained a mention of Tilbury Foster </s>
<s> Sally's patience broke down at this point, and he said, resentfully: "Damn his livers, he's immortal" </s>

<s> I know you do not mean any harm or any irreverence, poor boy, but you can't seem to open your mouth without letting out things to make a person shudder </s>

<s> For you and for all of us </s>
<s> Once I had no fear of the thunder, but now when I hear it I--" Her voice broke, and she began to cry, and could not finish </s>
<s> The sight of this smote Sally to the heart and he took her in his arms and petted her and comforted her and promised better conduct, and upbraided himself and remorsefully pleaded for forgiveness </s>
<s> And he was in earnest, and sorry for what he had done and ready for any sacrifice that could make up for it </s>
<s> And so, in privacy, he thought long and deeply over the matter, resolving to do what should seem best </s>
<s> It was easy to PROMISE reform; indeed he had already promised it </s>
<s> But would that do any real good, any permanent good </s>
<s> No, it would be but temporary--he knew his weakness, and confessed it to himself with sorrow--he could not keep the promise </s>
<s> Something surer and better must be devised; and he devised it </s>
<s> At cost of precious money which he had long been saving up, shilling by shilling, he put a lightning-rod on the house </s>
<s> At a subsequent time he relapsed </s>
<s> What miracles habit can do </s>
<s> and how quickly and how easily habits are acquired--both trifling habits and habits which profoundly change us </s>
<s> If by accident we wake at two in the morning a couple of nights in succession, we have need to be uneasy, for another repetition can turn the accident into a habit; and a month's dallying with whiskey--but we all know these commonplace facts </s>
<s> The castle-building habit, the day-dreaming habit--how it grows </s>
<s> what a luxury it becomes; how we fly to its enchantments at every idle moment, how we revel in them, steep our souls in them, intoxicate ourselves with their beguiling fantasies--oh yes, and how soon and how easily our dream life and our material life become so intermingled and so fused together that we can't quite tell which is which, any more </s>
<s> By and by Aleck subscribed to a Chicago daily and for the WALL STREET POINTER </s>

<s> Without added expense he could have left us far above desire of increase, far above the temptation to speculate, and a kinder soul would have done it; but in him was no generous spirit, no pity, no--" A DOG'S TALE CHAPTER I My father was a St </s>
<s> Bernard, my mother was a collie, but I am a Presbyterian </s>
<s> This is what my mother told me, I do not know these nice distinctions myself </s>
<s> To me they are only fine large words meaning nothing </s>
<s> My mother had a fondness for such; she liked to say them, and see other dogs look surprised and envious, as wondering how she got so much education </s>
<s> But, indeed, it was not real education; it was only show: she got the words by listening in the dining-room and drawing-room when there was company, and by going with the children to Sunday-school and listening there; and whenever she heard a large word she said it over to herself many times, and so was able to keep it until there was a dogmatic gathering in the neighborhood, then she would get it off, and surprise and distress them all, from pocket-pup to mastiff, which rewarded her for all her trouble </s>
<s> If there was a stranger he was nearly sure to be suspicious, and when he got his breath again he would ask her what it meant </s>
<s> And she always told him </s>
<s> He was never expecting this but thought he would catch her; so when she told him, he was the one that looked ashamed, whereas he had thought it was going to be she </s>
<s> The others were always waiting for this, and glad of it and proud of her, for they knew what was going to happen, because they had had experience </s>
<s> When she told the meaning of a big word they were all so taken up with admiration that it never occurred to any dog to doubt if it was the right one; and that was natural, because, for one thing, she answered up so promptly that it seemed like a dictionary speaking, and for another thing, where could they find out whether it was right or not </s>
<s> for she was the only cultivated dog there was </s>
<s> By and by, when I was older, she brought home the word Unintellectual, one time, and worked it pretty hard all the week at different gatherings, making much unhappiness and despondency; and it was at this time that I noticed that during that week she was asked for the meaning at eight different assemblages, and flashed out a fresh definition every time, which showed me that she had more presence of mind than culture, though I said nothing, of course </s>
<s> She had one word which she always kept on hand, and ready, like a life-preserver, a kind of emergency word to strap on when she was likely to get washed overboard in a sudden way--that was the word Synonymous </s>
<s> When she happened to fetch out a long word which had had its day weeks before and its prepared meanings gone to her dump-pile, if there was a stranger there of course it knocked him groggy for a couple of minutes, then he would come to, and by that time she would be away down wind on another tack, and not expecting anything; so when he'd hail and ask her to cash in, I (the only dog on the inside of her game) could see her canvas flicker a moment--but only just a moment--then it would belly out taut and full, and she would say, as calm as a summer's day, "It's synonymous with supererogation," or some godless long reptile of a word like that, and go placidly about and skim away on the next tack, perfectly comfortable, you know, and leave that stranger looking profane and embarrassed, and the initiated slatting the floor with their tails in unison and their faces transfigured with a holy joy </s>
<s> And it was the same with phrases </s>
<s> She would drag home a whole phrase, if it had a grand sound, and play it six nights and two matinees, and explain it a new way every time--which she had to, for all she cared for was the phrase; she wasn't interested in what it meant, and knew those dogs hadn't wit enough to catch her, anyway </s>
<s> Yes, she was a daisy </s>
<s> She got so she wasn't afraid of anything, she had such confidence in the ignorance of those creatures </s>
<s> She even brought anecdotes that she had heard the family and the dinner-guests laugh and shout over; and as a rule she got the nub of one chestnut hitched onto another chestnut, where, of course, it didn't fit and hadn't any point; and when she delivered the nub she fell over and rolled on the floor and laughed and barked in the most insane way, while I could see that she was wondering to herself why it didn't seem as funny as it did when she first heard it </s>
<s> But no harm was done; the others rolled and barked too, privately ashamed of themselves for not seeing the point, and never suspecting that the fault was not with them and there wasn't any to see </s>
<s> You can see by these things that she was of a rather vain and frivolous character; still, she had virtues, and enough to make up, I think </s>
<s> She had a kind heart and gentle ways, and never harbored resentments for injuries done her, but put them easily out of her mind and forgot them; and she taught her children her kindly way, and from her we learned also to be brave and prompt in time of danger, and not to run away, but face the peril that threatened friend or stranger, and help him the best we could without stopping to think what the cost might be to us </s>
<s> And she taught us not by words only, but by example, and that is the best way and the surest and the most lasting </s>
<s> Why, the brave things she did, the splendid things </s>
<s> she was just a soldier; and so modest about it--well, you couldn't help admiring her, and you couldn't help imitating her; not even a King Charles spaniel could remain entirely despicable in her society </s>
<s> So, as you see, there was more to her than her education </s>
<s> CHAPTER II When I was well grown, at last, I was sold and taken away, and I never saw her again </s>
<s> She was broken-hearted, and so was I, and we cried; but she comforted me as well as she could, and said we were sent into this world for a wise and good purpose, and must do our duties without repining, take our life as we might find it, live it for the best good of others, and never mind about the results; they were not our affair </s>
<s> She said men who did like this would have a noble and beautiful reward by and by in another world, and although we animals would not go there, to do well and right without reward would give to our brief lives a worthiness and dignity which in itself would be a reward </s>
<s> She had gathered these things from time to time when she had gone to the Sunday-school with the children, and had laid them up in her memory more carefully than she had done with those other words and phrases; and she had studied them deeply, for her good and ours </s>
<s> One may see by this that she had a wise and thoughtful head, for all there was so much lightness and vanity in it </s>
<s> So we said our farewells, and looked our last upon each other through our tears; and the last thing she said--keeping it for the last to make me remember it the better, I think--was, "In memory of me, when there is a time of danger to another do not think of yourself, think of your mother, and do as she would do" </s>
<s> Do you think I could forget that </s>
<s> No </s>
<s> CHAPTER III It was such a charming home!--my new one; a fine great house, with pictures, and delicate decorations, and rich furniture, and no gloom anywhere, but all the wilderness of dainty colors lit up with flooding sunshine; and the spacious grounds around it, and the great garden--oh, greensward, and noble trees, and flowers, no end </s>
<s> And I was the same as a member of the family; and they loved me, and petted me, and did not give me a new name, but called me by my old one that was dear to me because my mother had given it me--Aileen Mavoureen </s>
<s> She got it out of a song; and the Grays knew that song, and said it was a beautiful name </s>
<s> Mrs Gray was thirty, and so sweet and so lovely, you cannot imagine it; and Sadie was ten, and just like her mother, just a darling slender little copy of her, with auburn tails down her back, and short frocks; and the baby was a year old, and plump and dimpled, and fond of me, and never could get enough of hauling on my tail, and hugging me, and laughing out its innocent happiness; and Mr Gray was thirty-eight, and tall and slender and handsome, a little bald in front, alert, quick in his movements, business-like, prompt, decided, unsentimental, and with that kind of trim-chiseled face that just seems to glint and sparkle with frosty intellectuality </s>
<s> He was a renowned scientist </s>
<s> I do not know what the word means, but my mother would know how to use it and get effects </s>
<s> She would know how to depress a rat-terrier with it and make a lap-dog look sorry he came </s>
<s> But that is not the best one; the best one was Laboratory </s>
<s> My mother could organize a Trust on that one that would skin the tax-collars off the whole herd </s>
<s> The laboratory was not a book, or a picture, or a place to wash your hands in, as the college president's dog said--no, that is the lavatory; the laboratory is quite different, and is filled with jars, and bottles, and electrics, and wires, and strange machines; and every week other scientists came there and sat in the place, and used the machines, and discussed, and made what they called experiments and discoveries; and often I came, too, and stood around and listened, and tried to learn, for the sake of my mother, and in loving memory of her, although it was a pain to me, as realizing what she was losing out of her life and I gaining nothing at all; for try as I might, I was never able to make anything out of it at all </s>
<s> Other times I lay on the floor in the mistress's work-room and slept, she gently using me for a foot-stool, knowing it pleased me, for it was a caress; other times I spent an hour in the nursery, and got well tousled and made happy; other times I watched by the crib there, when the baby was asleep and the nurse out for a few minutes on the baby's affairs; other times I romped and raced through the grounds and the garden with Sadie till we were tired out, then slumbered on the grass in the shade of a tree while she read her book; other times I went visiting among the neighbor dogs--for there were some most pleasant ones not far away, and one very handsome and courteous and graceful one, a curly-haired Irish setter by the name of Robin Adair, who was a Presbyterian like me, and belonged to the Scotch minister </s>
<s> The servants in our house were all kind to me and were fond of me, and so, as you see, mine was a pleasant life </s>

<s> It was the dearest little waddling thing, and so smooth and soft and velvety, and had such cunning little awkward paws, and such affectionate eyes, and such a sweet and innocent face; and it made me so proud to see how the children and their mother adored it, and fondled it, and exclaimed over every little wonderful thing it did </s>
<s> It did seem to me that life was just too lovely to-- Then came the winter </s>
<s> One day I was standing a watch in the nursery </s>
<s> That is to say, I was asleep on the bed </s>
<s> The baby was asleep in the crib, which was alongside the bed, on the side next the fireplace </s>
<s> It was the kind of crib that has a lofty tent over it made of gauzy stuff that you can see through </s>
<s> The nurse was out, and we two sleepers were alone </s>
<s> A spark from the wood-fire was shot out, and it lit on the slope of the tent </s>

<s> Before I could think, I sprang to the floor in my fright, and in a second was half-way to the door; but in the next half-second my mother's farewell was sounding in my ears, and I was back on the bed again., I reached my head through the flames and dragged the baby out by the waist-band, and tugged it along, and we fell to the floor together in a cloud of smoke; I snatched a new hold, and dragged the screaming little creature along and out at the door and around the bend of the hall, and was still tugging away, all excited and happy and proud, when the master's voice shouted: "Begone you cursed beast" </s>

<s> I remember my mother pulling it on a kennel once, and explaining it in that way, but didn't say what agriculture was, except that it was synonymous with intramural incandescence; and a dozen times a day Mrs Gray and Sadie would tell the tale to new-comers, and say I risked my life to say the baby's, and both of us had burns to prove it, and then the company would pass me around and pet me and exclaim about me, and you could see the pride in the eyes of Sadie and her mother; and when the people wanted to know what made me limp, they looked ashamed and changed the subject, and sometimes when people hunted them this way and that way with questions about it, it looked to me as if they were going to cry </s>

<s> A CURE FOR THE BLUES By courtesy of Mr Cable I came into possession of a singular book eight or ten years ago </s>
<s> It is likely that mine is now the only copy in existence </s>
<s> Its title-page, unabbreviated, reads as follows: "The Enemy Conquered; or, Love Triumphant </s>
<s> By G </s>
<s> Ragsdale McClintock, (1) author of 'An Address,' etc, delivered at Sunflower Hill, South Carolina, and member of the Yale Law School </s>
<s> New Haven: published by T </s>
<s> H </s>
<s> Pease, 83 Chapel Street, 1845" </s>
<s> No one can take up this book and lay it down again unread </s>
<s> Whoever reads one line of it is caught, is chained; he has become the contented slave of its fascinations; and he will read and read, devour and devour, and will not let it go out of his hand till it is finished to the last line, though the house be on fire over his head </s>
<s> And after a first reading he will not throw it aside, but will keep it by him, with his Shakespeare and his Homer, and will take it up many and many a time, when the world is dark and his spirits are low, and be straightway cheered and refreshed </s>
<s> Yet this work has been allowed to lie wholly neglected, unmentioned, and apparently unregretted, for nearly half a century </s>
<s> The reader must not imagine that he is to find in it wisdom, brilliancy, fertility of invention, ingenuity of construction, excellence of form, purity of style, perfection of imagery, truth to nature, clearness of statement, humanly possible situations, humanly possible people, fluent narrative, connected sequence of events--or philosophy, or logic, or sense </s>
<s> No; the rich, deep, beguiling charm of the book lies in the total and miraculous ABSENCE from it of all these qualities--a charm which is completed and perfected by the evident fact that the author, whose naive innocence easily and surely wins our regard, and almost our worship, does not know that they are absent, does not even suspect that they are absent </s>
<s> When read by the light of these helps to an understanding of the situation, the book is delicious--profoundly and satisfyingly delicious </s>
<s> I call it a book because the author calls it a book, I call it a work because he calls it a work; but, in truth, it is merely a duodecimo pamphlet of thirty-one pages </s>
<s> It was written for fame and money, as the author very frankly--yes, and very hopefully, too, poor fellow--says in his preface </s>
<s> The money never came--no penny of it ever came; and how long, how pathetically long, the fame has been deferred--forty-seven years </s>
<s> He was young then, it would have been so much to him then; but will he care for it now </s>
<s> As time is measured in America, McClintock's epoch is antiquity </s>
<s> In his long-vanished day the Southern author had a passion for "eloquence"; it was his pet, his darling </s>
<s> He would be eloquent, or perish </s>
<s> And he recognized only one kind of eloquence--the lurid, the tempestuous, the volcanic </s>
<s> He liked words--big words, fine words, grand words, rumbling, thundering, reverberating words; with sense attaching if it could be got in without marring the sound, but not otherwise </s>
<s> He loved to stand up before a dazed world, and pour forth flame and smoke and lava and pumice-stone into the skies, and work his subterranean thunders, and shake himself with earthquakes, and stench himself with sulphur fumes </s>
<s> If he consumed his own fields and vineyards, that was a pity, yes; but he would have his eruption at any cost </s>
<s> Mr McClintock's eloquence--and he is always eloquent, his crater is always spouting--is of the pattern common to his day, but he departs from the custom of the time in one respect: his brethren allowed sense to intrude when it did not mar the sound, but he does not allow it to intrude at all </s>
<s> For example, consider this figure, which he used in the village "Address" referred to with such candid complacency in the title-page above quoted--"like the topmost topaz of an ancient tower" </s>
<s> Please read it again; contemplate it; measure it; walk around it; climb up it; try to get at an approximate realization of the size of it </s>
<s> Is the fellow to that to be found in literature, ancient or modern, foreign or domestic, living or dead, drunk or sober </s>
<s> One notices how fine and grand it sounds </s>
<s> We know that if it was loftily uttered, it got a noble burst of applause from the villagers; yet there isn't a ray of sense in it, or meaning to it </s>
<s> McClintock finished his education at Yale in 1843, and came to Hartford on a visit that same year </s>
<s> I have talked with men who at that time talked with him, and felt of him, and knew he was real </s>
<s> One needs to remember that fact and to keep fast hold of it; it is the only way to keep McClintock's book from undermining one's faith in McClintock's actuality </s>
<s> As to the book </s>
<s> The first four pages are devoted to an inflamed eulogy of Woman--simply woman in general, or perhaps as an institution--wherein, among other compliments to her details, he pays a unique one to her voice </s>
<s> He says it "fills the breast with fond alarms, echoed by every rill" </s>
<s> It sounds well enough, but it is not true </s>
<s> After the eulogy he takes up his real work and the novel begins </s>
<s> It begins in the woods, near the village of Sunflower Hill </s>
<s> Brightening clouds seemed to rise from the mist of the fair Chattahoochee, to spread their beauty over the thick forest, to guide the hero whose bosom beats with aspirations to conquer the enemy that would tarnish his name, and to win back the admiration of his long-tried friend </s>
<s> It seems a general remark, but it is not general; the hero mentioned is the to-be hero of the book; and in this abrupt fashion, and without name or description, he is shoveled into the tale </s>
<s> "With aspirations to conquer the enemy that would tarnish his name" is merely a phrase flung in for the sake of the sound--let it not mislead the reader </s>
<s> No one is trying to tarnish this person; no one has thought of it </s>
<s> The rest of the sentence is also merely a phrase; the man has no friend as yet, and of course has had no chance to try him, or win back his admiration, or disturb him in any other way </s>
<s> The hero climbs up over "Sawney's Mountain," and down the other side, making for an old Indian "castle"--which becomes "the red man's hut" in the next sentence; and when he gets there at last, he "surveys with wonder and astonishment" the invisible structure, "which time has buried in the dust, and thought to himself his happiness was not yet complete" </s>
<s> One doesn't know why it wasn't, nor how near it came to being complete, nor what was still wanting to round it up and make it so </s>
<s> Maybe it was the Indian; but the book does not say </s>
<s> At this point we have an episode: Beside the shore of the brook sat a young man, about eighteen or twenty, who seemed to be reading some favorite book, and who had a remarkably noble countenance--eyes which betrayed more than a common mind </s>
<s> This of course made the youth a welcome guest, and gained him friends in whatever condition of his life he might be placed </s>
<s> The traveler observed that he was a well-built figure which showed strength and grace in every movement </s>
<s> He accordingly addressed him in quite a gentlemanly manner, and inquired of him the way to the village </s>

<s> There is a strange sort of originality about McClintock; he imitates other people's styles, but nobody can imitate his, not even an idiot </s>
<s> Other people can be windy, but McClintock blows a gale; other people can blubber sentiment, but McClintock spews it; other people can mishandle metaphors, but only McClintock knows how to make a business of it </s>

<s> I begin this little work with an eulogy upon woman, who has ever been distinguished for her perseverance, her constancy, and her devoted attention to those upon whom she has been pleased to place her AFFECTIONS </s>
<s> Many have been the themes upon which writers and public speakers have dwelt with intense and increasing interest </s>
<s> Among these delightful themes stands that of woman, the balm to all our sighs and disappointments, and the most pre-eminent of all other topics </s>
<s> Here the poet and orator have stood and gazed with wonder and with admiration; they have dwelt upon her innocence, the ornament of all her virtues </s>
<s> First viewing her external charms, such as set forth in her form and benevolent countenance, and then passing to the deep hidden springs of loveliness and disinterested devotion </s>
<s> In every clime, and in every age, she has been the pride of her NATION </s>
<s> Her watchfulness is untiring; she who guarded the sepulcher was the first to approach it, and the last to depart from its awful yet sublime scene </s>
<s> Even here, in this highly favored land, we look to her for the security of our institutions, and for our future greatness as a nation </s>
<s> But, strange as it may appear, woman's charms and virtues are but slightly appreciated by thousands </s>
<s> Those who should raise the standard of female worth, and paint her value with her virtues, in living colors, upon the banners that are fanned by the zephyrs of heaven, and hand them down to posterity as emblematical of a rich inheritance, do not properly estimate them </s>
<s> Man is not sensible, at all times, of the nature and the emotions which bear that name; he does not understand, he will not comprehend; his intelligence has not expanded to that degree of glory which drinks in the vast revolution of humanity, its end, its mighty destination, and the causes which operated, and are still operating, to produce a more elevated station, and the objects which energize and enliven its consummation </s>
<s> This he is a stranger to; he is not aware that woman is the recipient of celestial love, and that man is dependent upon her to perfect his character; that without her, philosophically and truly speaking, the brightest of his intelligence is but the coldness of a winter moon, whose beams can produce no fruit, whose solar light is not its own, but borrowed from the great dispenser of effulgent beauty </s>
<s> We have no disposition in the world to flatter the fair sex, we would raise them above those dastardly principles which only exist in little souls, contracted hearts, and a distracted brain </s>
<s> Often does she unfold herself in all her fascinating loveliness, presenting the most captivating charms; yet we find man frequently treats such purity of purpose with indifference </s>
<s> Why does he do it </s>
<s> Why does he baffle that which is inevitably the source of his better days </s>
<s> Is he so much of a stranger to those excellent qualities as not to appreciate woman, as not to have respect to her dignity </s>
<s> Since her art and beauty first captivated man, she has been his delight and his comfort; she has shared alike in his misfortunes and in his prosperity </s>
<s> Whenever the billows of adversity and the tumultuous waves of trouble beat high, her smiles subdue their fury </s>
<s> Should the tear of sorrow and the mournful sigh of grief interrupt the peace of his mind, her voice removes them all, and she bends from her circle to encourage him onward </s>
<s> When darkness would obscure his mind, and a thick cloud of gloom would bewilder its operations, her intelligent eye darts a ray of streaming light into his heart </s>
<s> Mighty and charming is that disinterested devotion which she is ever ready to exercise toward man, not waiting till the last moment of his danger, but seeks to relieve him in his early afflictions </s>
<s> It gushes forth from the expansive fullness of a tender and devoted heart, where the noblest, the purest, and the most elevated and refined feelings are matured and developed in those may kind offices which invariably make her character </s>
<s> In the room of sorrow and sickness, this unequaled characteristic may always been seen, in the performance of the most charitable acts; nothing that she can do to promote the happiness of him who she claims to be her protector will be omitted; all is invigorated by the animating sunbeams which awaken the heart to songs of gaiety </s>

<s> THE CALIFORNIAN'S TALE Thirty-five years ago I was out prospecting on the Stanislaus, tramping all day long with pick and pan and horn, and washing a hatful of dirt here and there, always expecting to make a rich strike, and never doing it </s>
<s> It was a lovely region, woodsy, balmy, delicious, and had once been populous, long years before, but now the people had vanished and the charming paradise was a solitude </s>
<s> They went away when the surface diggings gave out </s>
<s> In one place, where a busy little city with banks and newspapers and fire companies and a mayor and aldermen had been, was nothing but a wide expanse of emerald turf, with not even the faintest sign that human life had ever been present there </s>
<s> This was down toward Tuttletown </s>
<s> In the country neighborhood thereabouts, along the dusty roads, one found at intervals the prettiest little cottage homes, snug and cozy, and so cobwebbed with vines snowed thick with roses that the doors and windows were wholly hidden from sight--sign that these were deserted homes, forsaken years ago by defeated and disappointed families who could neither sell them nor give them away </s>
<s> Now and then, half an hour apart, one came across solitary log cabins of the earliest mining days, built by the first gold-miners, the predecessors of the cottage-builders </s>
<s> In some few cases these cabins were still occupied; and when this was so, you could depend upon it that the occupant was the very pioneer who had built the cabin; and you could depend on another thing, too--that he was there because he had once had his opportunity to go home to the States rich, and had not done it; had rather lost his wealth, and had then in his humiliation resolved to sever all communication with his home relatives and friends, and be to them thenceforth as one dead </s>
<s> Round about California in that day were scattered a host of these living dead men--pride-smitten poor fellows, grizzled and old at forty, whose secret thoughts were made all of regrets and longings--regrets for their wasted lives, and longings to be out of the struggle and done with it all </s>
<s> It was a lonesome land </s>
<s> Not a sound in all those peaceful expanses of grass and woods but the drowsy hum of insects; no glimpse of man or beast; nothing to keep up your spirits and make you glad to be alive </s>
<s> And so, at last, in the early part of the afternoon, when I caught sight of a human creature, I felt a most grateful uplift </s>
<s> This person was a man about forty-five years old, and he was standing at the gate of one of those cozy little rose-clad cottages of the sort already referred to </s>
<s> However, this one hadn't a deserted look; it had the look of being lived in and petted and cared for and looked after; and so had its front yard, which was a garden of flowers, abundant, gay, and flourishing </s>
<s> I was invited in, of course, and required to make myself at home--it was the custom of the country </s>
<s> It was delightful to be in such a place, after long weeks of daily and nightly familiarity with miners' cabins--with all which this implies of dirt floor, never-made beds, tin plates and cups, bacon and beans and black coffee, and nothing of ornament but war pictures from the Eastern illustrated papers tacked to the log walls </s>
<s> That was all hard, cheerless, materialistic desolation, but here was a nest which had aspects to rest the tired eye and refresh that something in one's nature which, after long fasting, recognizes, when confronted by the belongings of art, howsoever cheap and modest they may be, that it has unconsciously been famishing and now has found nourishment </s>
<s> I could not have believed that a rag carpet could feast me so, and so content me; or that there could be such solace to the soul in wall-paper and framed lithographs, and bright-colored tidies and lamp-mats, and Windsor chairs, and varnished what-nots, with sea-shells and books and china vases on them, and the score of little unclassifiable tricks and touches that a woman's hand distributes about a home, which one sees without knowing he sees them, yet would miss in a moment if they were taken away </s>
<s> The delight that was in my heart showed in my face, and the man saw it and was pleased; saw it so plainly that he answered it as if it had been spoken </s>
<s> "All her work," he said, caressingly; "she did it all herself--every bit," and he took the room in with a glance which was full of affectionate worship </s>
<s> One of those soft Japanese fabrics with which women drape with careful negligence the upper part of a picture-frame was out of adjustment </s>
<s> He noticed it, and rearranged it with cautious pains, stepping back several times to gauge the effect before he got it to suit him </s>
<s> Then he gave it a light finishing pat or two with his hand, and said: "She always does that </s>
<s> You can't tell just what it lacks, but it does lack something until you've done that--you can see it yourself after it's done, but that is all you know; you can't find out the law of it </s>
<s> It's like the finishing pats a mother gives the child's hair after she's got it combed and brushed, I reckon </s>
<s> I've seen her fix all these things so much that I can do them all just her way, though I don't know the law of any of them </s>

<s> A HELPLESS SITUATION Once or twice a year I get a letter of a certain pattern, a pattern that never materially changes, in form and substance, yet I cannot get used to that letter--it always astonishes me </s>
<s> It affects me as the locomotive always affects me: I saw to myself, "I have seen you a thousand times, you always look the same way, yet you are always a wonder, and you are always impossible; to contrive you is clearly beyond human genius--you can't exist, you don't exist, yet here you are" </s>
<s> I have a letter of that kind by me, a very old one </s>
<s> I yearn to print it, and where is the harm </s>
<s> The writer of it is dead years ago, no doubt, and if I conceal her name and address--her this-world address--I am sure her shade will not mind </s>
<s> And with it I wish to print the answer which I wrote at the time but probably did not send </s>
<s> If it went--which is not likely--it went in the form of a copy, for I find the original still here, pigeonholed with the said letter </s>
<s> To that kind of letters we all write answers which we do not send, fearing to hurt where we have no desire to hurt; I have done it many a time, and this is doubtless a case of the sort </s>

<s> A TELEPHONIC CONVERSATION Consider that a conversation by telephone--when you are simply siting by and not taking any part in that conversation--is one of the solemnest curiosities of modern life </s>

<s> EDWARD MILLS AND GEORGE BENTON: A TALE These two were distantly related to each other--seventh cousins, or something of that sort </s>
<s> While still babies they became orphans, and were adopted by the Brants, a childless couple, who quickly grew very fond of them </s>
<s> The Brants were always saying: "Be pure, honest, sober, industrious, and considerate of others, and success in life is assured" </s>
<s> The children heard this repeated some thousands of times before they understood it; they could repeat it themselves long before they could say the Lord's Prayer; it was painted over the nursery door, and was about the first thing they learned to read </s>
<s> It was destined to be the unswerving rule of Edward Mills's life </s>
<s> Sometimes the Brants changed the wording a little, and said: "Be pure, honest, sober, industrious, considerate, and you will never lack friends" </s>
<s> Baby Mills was a comfort to everybody about him </s>
<s> When he wanted candy and could not have it, he listened to reason, and contented himself without it </s>
<s> When Baby Benton wanted candy, he cried for it until he got it </s>
<s> Baby Mills took care of his toys; Baby Benton always destroyed his in a very brief time, and then made himself so insistently disagreeable that, in order to have peace in the house, little Edward was persuaded to yield up his play-things to him </s>
<s> When the children were a little older, Georgie became a heavy expense in one respect: he took no care of his clothes; consequently, he shone frequently in new ones, with was not the case with Eddie </s>
<s> The boys grew apace </s>
<s> Eddie was an increasing comfort, Georgie an increasing solicitude </s>
<s> It was always sufficient to say, in answer to Eddie's petitions, "I would rather you would not do it"--meaning swimming, skating, picnicking, berrying, circusing, and all sorts of things which boys delight in </s>
<s> But NO answer was sufficient for Georgie; he had to be humored in his desires, or he would carry them with a high hand </s>
<s> Naturally, no boy got more swimming skating, berrying, and so forth than he; no body ever had a better time </s>
<s> The good Brants did not allow the boys to play out after nine in summer evenings; they were sent to bed at that hour; Eddie honorably remained, but Georgie usually slipped out of the window toward ten, and enjoyed himself until midnight </s>
<s> It seemed impossible to break Georgie of this bad habit, but the Brants managed it at last by hiring him, with apples and marbles, to stay in </s>
<s> The good Brants gave all their time and attention to vain endeavors to regulate Georgie; they said, with grateful tears in their eyes, that Eddie needed no efforts of theirs, he was so good, so considerate, and in all ways so perfect </s>
<s> By and by the boys were big enough to work, so they were apprenticed to a trade: Edward went voluntarily; George was coaxed and bribed </s>
<s> Edward worked hard and faithfully, and ceased to be an expense to the good Brants; they praised him, so did his master; but George ran away, and it cost Mr Brant both money and trouble to hunt him up and get him back </s>
<s> By and by he ran away again--more money and more trouble </s>
<s> He ran away a third time--and stole a few things to carry with him </s>
<s> Trouble and expense for Mr Brant once more; and, besides, it was with the greatest difficulty that he succeeded in persuading the master to let the youth go unprosecuted for the theft </s>
<s> Edward worked steadily along, and in time became a full partner in his master's business </s>
<s> George did not improve; he kept the loving hearts of his aged benefactors full of trouble, and their hands full of inventive activities to protect him from ruin </s>
<s> Edward, as a boy, had interested himself in Sunday-schools, debating societies, penny missionary affairs, anti-tobacco organizations, anti-profanity associations, and all such things; as a man, he was a quiet but steady and reliable helper in the church, the temperance societies, and in all movements looking to the aiding and uplifting of men </s>
<s> This excited no remark, attracted no attention--for it was his "natural bent" </s>
<s> Finally, the old people died </s>
<s> The will testified their loving pride in Edward, and left their little property to George--because he "needed it"; whereas, "owing to a bountiful Providence," such was not the case with Edward </s>
<s> The property was left to George conditionally: he must buy out Edward's partner with it; else it must go to a benevolent organization called the Prisoner's Friend Society </s>
<s> The old people left a letter, in which they begged their dear son Edward to take their place and watch over George, and help and shield him as they had done </s>
<s> Edward dutifully acquiesced, and George became his partner in the business </s>
<s> He was not a valuable partner: he had been meddling with drink before; he soon developed into a constant tippler now, and his flesh and eyes showed the fact unpleasantly </s>
<s> Edward had been courting a sweet and kindly spirited girl for some time </s>
<s> They loved each other dearly, and--But about this period George began to haunt her tearfully and imploringly, and at last she went crying to Edward, and said her high and holy duty was plain before her--she must not let her own selfish desires interfere with it: she must marry "poor George" and "reform him" </s>
<s> It would break her heart, she knew it would, and so on; but duty was duty </s>
<s> So she married George, and Edward's heart came very near breaking, as well as her own </s>
<s> However, Edward recovered, and married another girl--a very excellent one she was, too </s>
<s> Children came to both families </s>
<s> Mary did her honest best to reform her husband, but the contract was too large </s>
<s> George went on drinking, and by and by he fell to misusing her and the little ones sadly </s>
<s> A great many good people strove with George--they were always at it, in fact--but he calmly took such efforts as his due and their duty, and did not mend his ways </s>
<s> He added a vice, presently--that of secret gambling </s>
<s> He got deeply in debt; he borrowed money on the firm's credit, as quietly as he could, and carried this system so far and so successfully that one morning the sheriff took possession of the establishment, and the two cousins found themselves penniless </s>
<s> Times were hard, now, and they grew worse </s>
<s> Edward moved his family into a garret, and walked the streets day and night, seeking work </s>
<s> He begged for it, but it was really not to be had </s>
<s> He was astonished to see how soon his face became unwelcome; he was astonished and hurt to see how quickly the ancient interest which people had had in him faded out and disappeared </s>
<s> Still, he MUST get work; so he swallowed his chagrin, and toiled on in search of it </s>
<s> At last he got a job of carrying bricks up a ladder in a hod, and was a grateful man in consequence; but after that NOBODY knew him or cared anything about him </s>
<s> He was not able to keep up his dues in the various moral organizations to which he belonged, and had to endure the sharp pain of seeing himself brought under the disgrace of suspension </s>
<s> But the faster Edward died out of public knowledge and interest, the faster George rose in them </s>
<s> He was found lying, ragged and drunk, in the gutter one morning </s>
<s> A member of the Ladies' Temperance Refuge fished him out, took him in hand, got up a subscription for him, kept him sober a whole week, then got a situation for him </s>
<s> An account of it was published </s>
<s> General attention was thus drawn to the poor fellow, and a great many people came forward and helped him toward reform with their countenance and encouragement </s>
<s> He did not drink a drop for two months, and meantime was the pet of the good </s>
<s> Then he fell--in the gutter; and there was general sorrow and lamentation </s>
<s> But the noble sisterhood rescued him again </s>
<s> They cleaned him up, they fed him, they listened to the mournful music of his repentances, they got him his situation again </s>
<s> An account of this, also, was published, and the town was drowned in happy tears over the re-restoration of the poor beast and struggling victim of the fatal bowl </s>
<s> A grand temperance revival was got up, and after some rousing speeches had been made the chairman said, impressively: "We are not about to call for signers; and I think there is a spectacle in store for you which not many in this house will be able to view with dry eyes" </s>
<s> There was an eloquent pause, and then George Benton, escorted by a red-sashed detachment of the Ladies of the Refuge, stepped forward upon the platform and signed the pledge </s>
<s> The air was rent with applause, and everybody cried for joy </s>
<s> Everybody wrung the hand of the new convert when the meeting was over; his salary was enlarged next day; he was the talk of the town, and its hero </s>
<s> An account of it was published </s>
<s> George Benton fell, regularly, every three months, but was faithfully rescued and wrought with, every time, and good situations were found for him </s>
<s> Finally, he was taken around the country lecturing, as a reformed drunkard, and he had great houses and did an immense amount of good </s>
<s> He was so popular at home, and so trusted--during his sober intervals--that he was enabled to use the name of a principal citizen, and get a large sum of money at the bank </s>
<s> A mighty pressure was brought to bear to save him from the consequences of his forgery, and it was partially successful--he was "sent up" for only two years </s>
<s> When, at the end of a year, the tireless efforts of the benevolent were crowned with success, and he emerged from the penitentiary with a pardon in his pocket, the Prisoner's Friend Society met him at the door with a situation and a comfortable salary, and all the other benevolent people came forward and gave him advice, encouragement and help </s>
<s> Edward Mills had once applied to the Prisoner's Friend Society for a situation, when in dire need, but the question, "Have you been a prisoner" </s>
<s> made brief work of his case </s>
<s> While all these things were going on, Edward Mills had been quietly making head against adversity </s>
<s> He was still poor, but was in receipt of a steady and sufficient salary, as the respected and trusted cashier of a bank </s>
<s> George Benton never came near him, and was never heard to inquire about him </s>
<s> George got to indulging in long absences from the town; there were ill reports about him, but nothing definite </s>
<s> One winter's night some masked burglars forced their way into the bank, and found Edward Mills there alone </s>
<s> They commanded him to reveal the "combination," so that they could get into the safe </s>
<s> He refused </s>
<s> They threatened his life </s>
<s> He said his employers trusted him, and he could not be traitor to that trust </s>
<s> He could die, if he must, but while he lived he would be faithful; he would not yield up the "combination" </s>
<s> The burglars killed him </s>
<s> The detectives hunted down the criminals; the chief one proved to be George Benton </s>
<s> A wide sympathy was felt for the widow and orphans of the dead man, and all the newspapers in the land begged that all the banks in the land would testify their appreciation of the fidelity and heroism of the murdered cashier by coming forward with a generous contribution of money in aid of his family, now bereft of support </s>
<s> The result was a mass of solid cash amounting to upward of five hundred dollars--an average of nearly three-eights of a cent for each bank in the Union </s>
<s> The cashier's own bank testified its gratitude by endeavoring to show (but humiliatingly failed in it) that the peerless servant's accounts were not square, and that he himself had knocked his brains out with a bludgeon to escape detection and punishment </s>
<s> George Benton was arraigned for trial </s>
<s> Then everybody seemed to forget the widow and orphans in their solicitude for poor George </s>
<s> Everything that money and influence could do was done to save him, but it all failed; he was sentenced to death </s>
<s> Straightway the Governor was besieged with petitions for commutation or pardon; they were brought by tearful young girls; by sorrowful old maids; by deputations of pathetic widows; by shoals of impressive orphans </s>
<s> But no, the Governor--for once--would not yield </s>
<s> Now George Benton experienced religion </s>
<s> The glad news flew all around </s>
<s> From that time forth his cell was always full of girls and women and fresh flowers; all the day long there was prayer, and hymn-singing, and thanksgiving, and homilies, and tears, with never an interruption, except an occasional five-minute intermission for refreshments </s>
<s> This sort of thing continued up to the very gallows, and George Benton went proudly home, in the black cap, before a wailing audience of the sweetest and best that the region could produce </s>
<s> His grave had fresh flowers on it every day, for a while, and the head-stone bore these words, under a hand pointing aloft: "He has fought the good fight" </s>
<s> The brave cashier's head-stone has this inscription: "Be pure, honest, sober, industrious, considerate, and you will never--" Nobody knows who gave the order to leave it that way, but it was so given </s>
<s> The cashier's family are in stringent circumstances, now, it is said; but no matter; a lot of appreciative people, who were not willing that an act so brave and true as his should go unrewarded, have collected forty-two thousand dollars--and built a Memorial Church with it </s>
<s> THE FIVE BOONS OF LIFE Chapter I In the morning of life came a good fairy with her basket, and said: "Here are gifts </s>
<s> Take one, leave the others </s>
<s> And be wary, chose wisely; oh, choose wisely </s>
<s> for only one of them is valuable" </s>
<s> The gifts were five: Fame, Love, Riches, Pleasure, Death </s>
<s> The youth said, eagerly: "There is no need to consider"; and he chose Pleasure </s>
<s> He went out into the world and sought out the pleasures that youth delights in </s>
<s> But each in its turn was short-lived and disappointing, vain and empty; and each, departing, mocked him </s>
<s> In the end he said: "These years I have wasted </s>
<s> If I could but choose again, I would choose wisely" </s>
<s> Chapter II The fairy appeared, and said: "Four of the gifts remain </s>
<s> Choose once more; and oh, remember--time is flying, and only one of them is precious" </s>
<s> The man considered long, then chose Love; and did not mark the tears that rose in the fairy's eyes </s>
<s> After many, many years the man sat by a coffin, in an empty home </s>
<s> And he communed with himself, saying: "One by one they have gone away and left me; and now she lies here, the dearest and the last </s>
<s> Desolation after desolation has swept over me; for each hour of happiness the treacherous trader, Love, as sold me I have paid a thousand hours of grief </s>
<s> Out of my heart of hearts I curse him" </s>
<s> Chapter III "Choose again" </s>
<s> It was the fairy speaking </s>
<s> "The years have taught you wisdom--surely it must be so </s>
<s> Three gifts remain </s>
<s> Only one of them has any worth--remember it, and choose warily" </s>
<s> The man reflected long, then chose Fame; and the fairy, sighing, went her way </s>
<s> Years went by and she came again, and stood behind the man where he sat solitary in the fading day, thinking </s>
<s> And she knew his thought: "My name filled the world, and its praises were on every tongue, and it seemed well with me for a little while </s>
<s> How little a while it was </s>
<s> Then came envy; then detraction; then calumny; then hate; then persecution </s>
<s> Then derision, which is the beginning of the end </s>
<s> And last of all came pity, which is the funeral of fame </s>
<s> Oh, the bitterness and misery of renown </s>
<s> target for mud in its prime, for contempt and compassion in its decay" </s>
<s> Chapter IV "Chose yet again" </s>
<s> It was the fairy's voice </s>
<s> "Two gifts remain </s>
<s> And do not despair </s>
<s> In the beginning there was but one that was precious, and it is still here" </s>
<s> "Wealth--which is power </s>
<s> How blind I was" </s>
<s> said the man </s>
<s> "Now, at last, life will be worth the living </s>
<s> I will spend, squander, dazzle </s>
<s> These mockers and despisers will crawl in the dirt before me, and I will feed my hungry heart with their envy </s>
<s> I will have all luxuries, all joys, all enchantments of the spirit, all contentments of the body that man holds dear </s>
<s> I will buy, buy, buy </s>
<s> deference, respect, esteem, worship--every pinchbeck grace of life the market of a trivial world can furnish forth </s>
<s> I have lost much time, and chosen badly heretofore, but let that pass; I was ignorant then, and could but take for best what seemed so" </s>
<s> Three short years went by, and a day came when the man sat shivering in a mean garret; and he was gaunt and wan and hollow-eyed, and clothed in rags; and he was gnawing a dry crust and mumbling: "Curse all the world's gifts, for mockeries and gilded lies </s>
<s> And miscalled, every one </s>
<s> They are not gifts, but merely lendings </s>
<s> Pleasure, Love, Fame, Riches: they are but temporary disguises for lasting realities--Pain, Grief, Shame, Poverty </s>
<s> The fairy said true; in all her store there was but one gift which was precious, only one that was not valueless </s>
<s> How poor and cheap and mean I know those others now to be, compared with that inestimable one, that dear and sweet and kindly one, that steeps in dreamless and enduring sleep the pains that persecute the body, and the shames and griefs that eat the mind and heart </s>
<s> Bring it </s>
<s> I am weary, I would rest" </s>
<s> Chapter V The fairy came, bringing again four of the gifts, but Death was wanting </s>
<s> She said: "I gave it to a mother's pet, a little child </s>
<s> It was ignorant, but trusted me, asking me to choose for it </s>
<s> You did not ask me to choose" </s>
<s> "Oh, miserable me </s>
<s> What is left for me" </s>
<s> "What not even you have deserved: the wanton insult of Old Age" </s>
<s> THE FIRST WRITING-MACHINES From My Unpublished Autobiography Some days ago a correspondent sent in an old typewritten sheet, faded by age, containing the following letter over the signature of Mark Twain: "Hartford, March 10, 1875 </s>
<s> "Please do not use my name in any way </s>
<s> Please do not even divulge that fact that I own a machine </s>
<s> I have entirely stopped using the typewriter, for the reason that I never could write a letter with it to anybody without receiving a request by return mail that I would not only describe the machine, but state what progress I had made in the use of it, etc, etc I don't like to write letters, and so I don't want people to know I own this curiosity-breeding little joker" </s>
<s> A note was sent to Mr Clemens asking him if the letter was genuine and whether he really had a typewriter as long ago as that </s>
<s> Mr Clemens replied that his best answer is the following chapter from his unpublished autobiography: 1904 </s>
<s> VILLA QUARTO, FLORENCE, JANUARY </s>
<s> Dictating autobiography to a typewriter is a new experience for me, but it goes very well, and is going to save time and "language"--the kind of language that soothes vexation </s>
<s> I have dictated to a typewriter before--but not autobiography </s>
<s> Between that experience and the present one there lies a mighty gap--more than thirty years </s>
<s> It is sort of lifetime </s>
<s> In that wide interval much has happened--to the type-machine as well as to the rest of us </s>
<s> At the beginning of that interval a type-machine was a curiosity </s>
<s> The person who owned one was a curiosity, too </s>
<s> But now it is the other way about: the person who DOESN'T own one is a curiosity </s>
<s> I saw a type-machine for the first time in--what year </s>
<s> I suppose it was 1873--because Nasby was with me at the time, and it was in Boston </s>
<s> We must have been lecturing, or we could not have been in Boston, I take it </s>
<s> I quitted the platform that season </s>
<s> But never mind about that, it is no matter </s>
<s> Nasby and I saw the machine through a window, and went in to look at it </s>
<s> The salesman explained it to us, showed us samples of its work, and said it could do fifty-seven words a minute--a statement which we frankly confessed that we did not believe </s>
<s> So he put his type-girl to work, and we timed her by the watch </s>
<s> She actually did the fifty-seven in sixty seconds </s>
<s> We were partly convinced, but said it probably couldn't happen again </s>
<s> But it did </s>
<s> We timed the girl over and over again--with the same result always: she won out </s>
<s> She did her work on narrow slips of paper, and we pocketed them as fast as she turned them out, to show as curiosities </s>
<s> The price of the machine was one hundred and twenty-five dollars </s>
<s> I bought one, and we went away very much excited </s>
<s> At the hotel we got out our slips and were a little disappointed to find that they contained the same words </s>
<s> The girl had economized time and labor by using a formula which she knew by heart </s>
<s> However, we argued--safely enough--that the FIRST type-girl must naturally take rank with the first billiard-player: neither of them could be expected to get out of the game any more than a third or a half of what was in it </s>
<s> If the machine survived--IF it survived--experts would come to the front, by and by, who would double the girl's output without a doubt </s>
<s> They would do one hundred words a minute--my talking speed on the platform </s>
<s> That score has long ago been beaten </s>
<s> At home I played with the toy, repeated and repeating and repeated "The Boy stood on the Burning Deck," until I could turn that boy's adventure out at the rate of twelve words a minute; then I resumed the pen, for business, and only worked the machine to astonish inquiring visitors </s>
<s> They carried off many reams of the boy and his burning deck </s>
<s> By and by I hired a young woman, and did my first dictating (letters, merely), and my last until now </s>
<s> The machine did not do both capitals and lower case (as now), but only capitals </s>
<s> Gothic capitals they were, and sufficiently ugly </s>
<s> I remember the first letter I dictated, it was to Edward Bok, who was a boy then </s>
<s> I was not acquainted with him at that time </s>
<s> His present enterprising spirit is not new--he had it in that early day </s>
<s> He was accumulating autographs, and was not content with mere signatures, he wanted a whole autograph LETTER </s>
<s> I furnished it--in type-written capitals, SIGNATURE AND ALL </s>
<s> It was long; it was a sermon; it contained advice; also reproaches </s>
<s> I said writing was my TRADE, my bread-and-butter; I said it was not fair to ask a man to give away samples of his trade; would he ask the blacksmith for a horseshoe </s>
<s> would he ask the doctor for a corpse </s>
<s> Now I come to an important matter--as I regard it </s>
<s> In the year '74 the young woman copied a considerable part of a book of mine ON THE MACHINE </s>
<s> In a previous chapter of this Autobiography I have claimed that I was the first person in the world that ever had a telephone in the house for practical purposes; I will now claim--until dispossess--that I was the first person in the world to APPLY THE TYPE-MACHINE TO LITERATURE </s>
<s> That book must have been THE ADVENTURES OF TOM SAWYER </s>
<s> I wrote the first half of it in '72, the rest of it in '74 </s>
<s> My machinist type-copied a book for me in '74, so I concluded it was that one </s>
<s> That early machine was full of caprices, full of defects--devilish ones </s>
<s> It had as many immoralities as the machine of today has virtues </s>
<s> After a year or two I found that it was degrading my character, so I thought I would give it to Howells </s>
<s> He was reluctant, for he was suspicious of novelties and unfriendly toward them, and he remains so to this day </s>
<s> But I persuaded him </s>
<s> He had great confidence in me, and I got him to believe things about the machine that I did not believe myself </s>
<s> He took it home to Boston, and my morals began to improve, but his have never recovered </s>
<s> He kept it six months, and then returned it to me </s>
<s> I gave it away twice after that, but it wouldn't stay; it came back </s>
<s> Then I gave it to our coachman, Patrick McAleer, who was very grateful, because he did not know the animal, and thought I was trying to make him wiser and better </s>
<s> As soon as he got wiser and better he traded it to a heretic for a side-saddle which he could not use, and there my knowledge of its history ends </s>
<s> ITALIAN WITHOUT A MASTER It is almost a fortnight now that I am domiciled in a medieval villa in the country, a mile or two from Florence </s>
<s> I cannot speak the language; I am too old not to learn how, also too busy when I am busy, and too indolent when I am not; wherefore some will imagine that I am having a dull time of it </s>
<s> But it is not so </s>
<s> The "help" are all natives; they talk Italian to me, I answer in English; I do not understand them, they do not understand me, consequently no harm is done, and everybody is satisfied </s>
<s> In order to be just and fair, I throw in an Italian word when I have one, and this has a good influence </s>
<s> I get the word out of the morning paper </s>
<s> I have to use it while it is fresh, for I find that Italian words do not keep in this climate </s>
<s> They fade toward night, and next morning they are gone </s>

<s> During my first week in the deep and dreamy stillness of this woodsy and flowery place I was without news of the outside world, and was well content without it </s>

<s> The headline is a valuable thing </s>
<s> Necessarily we are all fond of murders, scandals, swindles, robberies, explosions, collisions, and all such things, when we knew the people, and when they are neighbors and friends, but when they are strangers we do not get any great pleasure out of them, as a rule </s>
<s> Now the trouble with an American paper is that it has no discrimination; it rakes the whole earth for blood and garbage, and the result is that you are daily overfed and suffer a surfeit </s>
<s> By habit you stow this muck every day, but you come by and by to take no vital interest in it--indeed, you almost get tired of it </s>

<s> The existing phrase-books are inadequate </s>
