<s> DIALOGUE 17 To Inform One'self of a Person How is that gentilman who you did speak by and by </s>
<s> Is a German </s>
<s> I did think him Englishman </s>
<s> He is of the Saxony side </s>
<s> He speak the french very well </s>
<s> Tough he is German, he speak so much well italyan, french, spanish and english, that among the Italyans, they believe him Italyan, he speak the frenche as the Frenches himselves </s>
<s> The Spanishesmen believe him Spanishing, and the Englishes, Englishman </s>
<s> It is difficult to enjoy well so much several languages </s>
<s> The last remark contains a general truth; but it ceases to be a truth when one contracts it and apples it to an individual--provided that that individual is the author of this book, Sehnor Pedro Carolino </s>
<s> I am sure I should not find it difficult "to enjoy well so much several languages"--or even a thousand of them--if he did the translating for me from the originals into his ostensible English </s>
<s> ADVICE TO LITTLE GIRLS Good little girls ought not to make mouths at their teachers for every trifling offense </s>
<s> This retaliation should only be resorted to under peculiarly aggravated circumstances </s>
<s> If you have nothing but a rag-doll stuffed with sawdust, while one of your more fortunate little playmates has a costly China one, you should treat her with a show of kindness nevertheless </s>
<s> And you ought not to attempt to make a forcible swap with her unless your conscience would justify you in it, and you know you are able to do it </s>
<s> You ought never to take your little brother's "chewing-gum" away from him by main force; it is better to rope him in with the promise of the first two dollars and a half you find floating down the river on a grindstone </s>
<s> In the artless simplicity natural to this time of life, he will regard it as a perfectly fair transaction </s>
<s> In all ages of the world this eminently plausible fiction has lured the obtuse infant to financial ruin and disaster </s>
<s> If at any time you find it necessary to correct your brother, do not correct him with mud--never, on any account, throw mud at him, because it will spoil his clothes </s>
<s> It is better to scald him a little, for then you obtain desirable results </s>
<s> You secure his immediate attention to the lessons you are inculcating, and at the same time your hot water will have a tendency to move impurities from his person, and possibly the skin, in spots </s>
<s> If your mother tells you to do a thing, it is wrong to reply that you won't </s>
<s> It is better and more becoming to intimate that you will do as she bids you, and then afterward act quietly in the matter according to the dictates of your best judgment </s>
<s> You should ever bear in mind that it is to your kind parents that you are indebted for your food, and for the privilege of staying home from school when you let on that you are sick </s>
<s> Therefore you ought to respect their little prejudices, and humor their little whims, and put up with their little foibles until they get to crowding you too much </s>
<s> Good little girls always show marked deference for the aged </s>
<s> You ought never to "sass" old people unless they "sass" you first </s>
<s> POST-MORTEM POETRY (1) In Philadelphia they have a custom which it would be pleasant to see adopted throughout the land </s>
<s> It is that of appending to published death-notices a little verse or two of comforting poetry </s>
<s> Any one who is in the habit of reading the daily Philadelphia LEDGER must frequently be touched by these plaintive tributes to extinguished worth </s>
<s> In Philadelphia, the departure of a child is a circumstance which is not more surely followed by a burial than by the accustomed solacing poesy in the PUBLIC LEDGER </s>
<s> In that city death loses half its terror because the knowledge of its presence comes thus disguised in the sweet drapery of verse </s>
<s> For instance, in a late LEDGER I find the following (I change the surname): DIED Hawks.--On the 17th inst., Clara, the daughter of Ephraim and Laura Hawks, aged 21 months and 2 days </s>
<s> That merry shout no more I hear, No laughing child I see, No little arms are around my neck, No feet upon my knee; No kisses drop upon my cheek, These lips are sealed to me </s>
<s> Dear Lord, how could I give Clara up To any but to Thee </s>
<s> A child thus mourned could not die wholly discontented </s>
<s> From the LEDGER of the same date I make the following extract, merely changing the surname, as before: Becket.--On Sunday morning, 19th inst., John P., infant son of George and Julia Becket, aged 1 year, 6 months, and 15 days </s>
<s> That merry shout no more I hear, No laughing child I see, No little arms are round my neck, No feet upon my knee; No kisses drop upon my cheek; These lips are sealed to me </s>
<s> Dear Lord, how could I give Johnnie up To any but to Thee </s>
<s> The similarity of the emotions as produced in the mourners in these two instances is remarkably evidenced by the singular similarity of thought which they experienced, and the surprising coincidence of language used by them to give it expression </s>
<s> In the same journal, of the same date, I find the following (surname suppressed, as before): Wagner.--On the 10th inst., Ferguson G., the son of William L </s>
<s> and Martha Theresa Wagner, aged 4 weeks and 1 day </s>
<s> That merry shout no more I hear, No laughing child I see, No little arms are round my neck, No feet upon my knee; No kisses drop upon my cheek, These lips are sealed to me </s>
<s> Dear Lord, how could I give Ferguson up To any but to Thee </s>
<s> It is strange what power the reiteration of an essentially poetical thought has upon one's feelings </s>
<s> When we take up the LEDGER and read the poetry about little Clara, we feel an unaccountable depression of the spirits </s>
<s> When we drift further down the column and read the poetry about little Johnnie, the depression and spirits acquires and added emphasis, and we experience tangible suffering </s>
<s> When we saunter along down the column further still and read the poetry about little Ferguson, the word torture but vaguely suggests the anguish that rends us </s>
<s> In the LEDGER (same copy referred to above) I find the following (I alter surname, as usual): Welch.--On the 5th inst., Mary C </s>
<s> Welch, wife of William B </s>
<s> Welch, and daughter of Catharine and George W </s>
<s> Markland, in the 29th year of her age </s>
<s> A mother dear, a mother kind, Has gone and left us all behind </s>
<s> Cease to weep, for tears are vain, Mother dear is out of pain </s>
<s> Farewell, husband, children dear, Serve thy God with filial fear, And meet me in the land above, Where all is peace, and joy, and love </s>
<s> What could be sweeter than that </s>
<s> No collection of salient facts (without reduction to tabular form) could be more succinctly stated than is done in the first stanza by the surviving relatives, and no more concise and comprehensive program of farewells, post-mortuary general orders, etc, could be framed in any form than is done in verse by deceased in the last stanza </s>
<s> These things insensibly make us wiser and tenderer, and better </s>
<s> Another extract: Ball.--On the morning of the 15th inst., Mary E., daughter of John and Sarah F </s>
<s> Ball </s>
<s> 'Tis sweet to rest in lively hope That when my change shall come Angels will hover round my bed, To waft my spirit home </s>
<s> The following is apparently the customary form for heads of families: Burns.--On the 20th inst., Michael Burns, aged 40 years </s>
<s> Dearest father, thou hast left us, Hear thy loss we deeply feel; But 'tis God that has bereft us, He can all our sorrows heal </s>
<s> Funeral at 2 o'clock sharp </s>
<s> There is something very simple and pleasant about the following, which, in Philadelphia, seems to be the usual form for consumptives of long standing </s>
<s> (It deplores four distinct cases in the single copy of the LEDGER which lies on the Memoranda editorial table): Bromley.--On the 29th inst., of consumption, Philip Bromley, in the 50th year of his age </s>
<s> Affliction sore long time he bore, Physicians were in vain-- Till God at last did hear him mourn, And eased him of his pain </s>
<s> That friend whom death from us has torn, We did not think so soon to part; An anxious care now sinks the thorn Still deeper in our bleeding heart </s>
<s> This beautiful creation loses nothing by repetition </s>
<s> On the contrary, the oftener one sees it in the LEDGER, the more grand and awe-inspiring it seems </s>
<s> With one more extract I will close: Doble.--On the 4th inst., Samuel Pervil Worthington Doble, aged 4 days </s>
<s> Our little Sammy's gone, His tiny spirit's fled; Our little boy we loved so dear Lies sleeping with the dead </s>
<s> A tear within a father's eye, A mother's aching heart, Can only tell the agony How hard it is to part </s>
<s> Could anything be more plaintive than that, without requiring further concessions of grammar </s>
<s> Could anything be likely to do more toward reconciling deceased to circumstances, and making him willing to go </s>
<s> Perhaps not </s>
<s> The power of song can hardly be estimated </s>
<s> There is an element about some poetry which is able to make even physical suffering and death cheerful things to contemplate and consummations to be desired </s>
<s> This element is present in the mortuary poetry of Philadelphia degree of development </s>
<s> The custom I have been treating of is one that should be adopted in all the cities of the land </s>
<s> It is said that once a man of small consequence died, and the Rev </s>
<s> T </s>
<s> K </s>
<s> Beecher was asked to preach the funeral sermon--a man who abhors the lauding of people, either dead or alive, except in dignified and simple language, and then only for merits which they actually possessed or possess, not merits which they merely ought to have possessed </s>
<s> The friends of the deceased got up a stately funeral </s>
<s> They must have had misgivings that the corpse might not be praised strongly enough, for they prepared some manuscript headings and notes in which nothing was left unsaid on that subject that a fervid imagination and an unabridged dictionary could compile, and these they handed to the minister as he entered the pulpit </s>
<s> They were merely intended as suggestions, and so the friends were filled with consternation when the minister stood in the pulpit and proceeded to read off the curious odds and ends in ghastly detail and in a loud voice </s>
<s> And their consternation solidified to petrification when he paused at the end, contemplated the multitude reflectively, and then said, impressively: "The man would be a fool who tried to add anything to that </s>
<s> Let us pray" </s>
<s> And with the same strict adhesion to truth it can be said that the man would be a fool who tried to add anything to the following transcendent obituary poem </s>
<s> There is something so innocent, so guileless, so complacent, so unearthly serene and self-satisfied about this peerless "hog-wash," that the man must be made of stone who can read it without a dulcet ecstasy creeping along his backbone and quivering in his marrow </s>
<s> There is no need to say that this poem is genuine and in earnest, for its proofs are written all over its face </s>
<s> An ingenious scribbler might imitate it after a fashion, but Shakespeare himself could not counterfeit it </s>
<s> It is noticeable that the country editor who published it did not know that it was a treasure and the most perfect thing of its kind that the storehouses and museums of literature could show </s>
<s> He did not dare to say no to the dread poet--for such a poet must have been something of an apparition--but he just shoveled it into his paper anywhere that came handy, and felt ashamed, and put that disgusted "Published by Request" over it, and hoped that his subscribers would overlook it or not feel an impulse to read it: (Published by Request) LINES Composed on the death of Samuel and Catharine Belknap's children by M </s>
<s> A </s>
<s> Glaze Friends and neighbors all draw near, And listen to what I have to say; And never leave your children dear When they are small, and go away </s>
<s> But always think of that sad fate, That happened in year of '63; Four children with a house did burn, Think of their awful agony </s>
<s> Their mother she had gone away, And left them there alone to stay; The house took fire and down did burn; Before their mother did return </s>
<s> Their piteous cry the neighbors heard, And then the cry of fire was given; But, ah </s>
<s> before they could them reach, Their little spirits had flown to heaven </s>
<s> Their father he to war had gone, And on the battle-field was slain; But little did he think when he went away, But what on earth they would meet again </s>
<s> The neighbors often told his wife Not to leave his children there, Unless she got some one to stay, And of the little ones take care </s>
<s> The oldest he was years not six, And the youngest only eleven months old, But often she had left them there alone, As, by the neighbors, I have been told </s>
<s> How can she bear to see the place </s>
<s> Where she so oft has left them there, Without a single one to look to them, Or of the little ones to take good care </s>
<s> Oh, can she look upon the spot, Whereunder their little burnt bones lay, But what she thinks she hears them say, ''Twas God had pity, and took us on high' </s>
<s> And there may she kneel down and pray, And ask God her to forgive; And she may lead a different life While she on earth remains to live </s>
<s> Her husband and her children too, God has took from pain and woe </s>
<s> May she reform and mend her ways, That she may also to them go </s>
<s> And when it is God's holy will, O, may she be prepared To meet her God and friends in peace, And leave this world of care </s>

<s> THE DANGER OF LYING IN BED The man in the ticket-office said: "Have an accident insurance ticket, also" </s>
<s> "No," I said, after studying the matter over a little </s>
<s> "No, I believe not; I am going to be traveling by rail all day today </s>
<s> However, tomorrow I don't travel </s>
<s> Give me one for tomorrow" </s>
<s> The man looked puzzled </s>
<s> He said: "But it is for accident insurance, and if you are going to travel by rail--" "If I am going to travel by rail I sha'n't need it </s>
<s> Lying at home in bed is the thing _I_ am afraid of" </s>
<s> I had been looking into this matter </s>
<s> Last year I traveled twenty thousand miles, almost entirely by rail; the year before, I traveled over twenty-five thousand miles, half by sea and half by rail; and the year before that I traveled in the neighborhood of ten thousand miles, exclusively by rail </s>
<s> I suppose if I put in all the little odd journeys here and there, I may say I have traveled sixty thousand miles during the three years I have mentioned </s>
<s> AND NEVER AN ACCIDENT </s>
<s> For a good while I said to myself every morning: "Now I have escaped thus far, and so the chances are just that much increased that I shall catch it this time </s>
<s> I will be shrewd, and buy an accident ticket" </s>
<s> And to a dead moral certainty I drew a blank, and went to bed that night without a joint started or a bone splintered </s>
<s> I got tired of that sort of daily bother, and fell to buying accident tickets that were good for a month </s>
<s> I said to myself, "A man CAN'T buy thirty blanks in one bundle" </s>
<s> But I was mistaken </s>
<s> There was never a prize in the the lot </s>

<s> I found plenty of people who had invested, but not an individual that had ever had an accident or made a cent </s>
<s> I stopped buying accident tickets and went to ciphering </s>
<s> The result was astounding </s>
<s> THE PERIL LAY NOT IN TRAVELING, BUT IN STAYING AT HOME </s>
<s> I hunted up statistics, and was amazed to find that after all the glaring newspaper headlines concerning railroad disasters, less than THREE HUNDRED people had really lost their lives by those disasters in the preceding twelve months </s>
<s> The Erie road was set down as the most murderous in the list </s>
<s> It had killed forty-six--or twenty-six, I do not exactly remember which, but I know the number was double that of any other road </s>
<s> But the fact straightway suggested itself that the Erie was an immensely long road, and did more business than any other line in the country; so the double number of killed ceased to be matter for surprise </s>
<s> By further figuring, it appeared that between New York and Rochester the Erie ran eight passenger-trains each way every day--16 altogether; and carried a daily average of 6,000 persons </s>
<s> That is about a million in six months--the population of New York City </s>
<s> Well, the Erie kills from 13 to 23 persons of ITS million in six months; and in the same time 13,000 of New York's million die in their beds </s>
<s> My flesh crept, my hair stood on end </s>
<s> "This is appalling" </s>
<s> I said </s>
<s> "The danger isn't in traveling by rail, but in trusting to those deadly beds </s>
<s> I will never sleep in a bed again" </s>
<s> I had figured on considerably less than one-half the length of the Erie road </s>
<s> It was plain that the entire road must transport at least eleven or twelve thousand people every day </s>
<s> There are many short roads running out of Boston that do fully half as much; a great many such roads </s>
<s> There are many roads scattered about the Union that do a prodigious passenger business </s>
<s> Therefore it was fair to presume that an average of 2,500 passengers a day for each road in the country would be almost correct </s>
<s> There are 846 railway lines in our country, and 846 times 2,500 are 2,115,000 </s>
<s> So the railways of America move more than two millions of people every day; six hundred and fifty millions of people a year, without counting the Sundays </s>
<s> They do that, too--there is no question about it; though where they get the raw material is clear beyond the jurisdiction of my arithmetic; for I have hunted the census through and through, and I find that there are not that many people in the United States, by a matter of six hundred and ten millions at the very least </s>
<s> They must use some of the same people over again, likely </s>
<s> San Francisco is one-eighth as populous as New York; there are 60 deaths a week in the former and 500 a week in the latter--if they have luck </s>
<s> That is 3,120 deaths a year in San Francisco, and eight times as many in New York--say about 25,000 or 26,000 </s>
<s> The health of the two places is the same </s>
<s> So we will let it stand as a fair presumption that this will hold good all over the country, and that consequently 25,000 out of every million of people we have must die every year </s>
<s> That amounts to one-fortieth of our total population </s>
<s> One million of us, then, die annually </s>
<s> Out of this million ten or twelve thousand are stabbed, shot, drowned, hanged, poisoned, or meet a similarly violent death in some other popular way, such as perishing by kerosene-lamp and hoop-skirt conflagrations, getting buried in coal-mines, falling off house-tops, breaking through church, or lecture-room floors, taking patent medicines, or committing suicide in other forms </s>
<s> The Erie railroad kills 23 to 46; the other 845 railroads kill an average of one-third of a man each; and the rest of that million, amounting in the aggregate to that appalling figure of 987,631 corpses, die naturally in their beds </s>
<s> You will excuse me from taking any more chances on those beds </s>
<s> The railroads are good enough for me </s>
<s> And my advice to all people is, Don't stay at home any more than you can help; but when you have GOT to stay at home a while, buy a package of those insurance tickets and sit up nights </s>
<s> You cannot be too cautious </s>
<s> (One can see now why I answered that ticket-agent in the manner recorded at the top of this sketch.) The moral of this composition is, that thoughtless people grumble more than is fair about railroad management in the United States </s>
<s> When we consider that every day and night of the year full fourteen thousand railway-trains of various kinds, freighted with life and armed with death, go thundering over the land, the marvel is, NOT that they kill three hundred human beings in a twelvemonth, but that they do not kill three hundred times three hundred </s>
<s> PORTRAIT OF KING WILLIAM III I never can look at those periodical portraits in THE GALAXY magazine without feeling a wild, tempestuous ambition to be an artist </s>
<s> I have seen thousands and thousands of pictures in my time--acres of them here and leagues of them in the galleries of Europe--but never any that moved me as these portraits do </s>
<s> There is a portrait of Monsignore Capel in the November number, now COULD anything be sweeter than that </s>
<s> And there was Bismarck's, in the October number; who can look at that without being purer and stronger and nobler for it </s>
<s> And Thurlow and Weed's picture in the September number; I would not have died without seeing that, no, not for anything this world can give </s>
<s> But look back still further and recall my own likeness as printed in the August number; if I had been in my grave a thousand years when that appeared, I would have got up and visited the artist </s>
<s> I sleep with all these portraits under my pillow every night, so that I can go on studying them as soon as the day dawns in the morning </s>
<s> I know them all as thoroughly as if I had made them myself; I know every line and mark about them </s>
<s> Sometimes when company are present I shuffle the portraits all up together, and then pick them out one by one and call their names, without referring to the printing on the bottom </s>
<s> I seldom make a mistake--never, when I am calm </s>
<s> I have had the portraits framed for a long time, waiting till my aunt gets everything ready for hanging them up in the parlor </s>
<s> But first one thing and then another interferes, and so the thing is delayed </s>
<s> Once she said they would have more of the peculiar kind of light they needed in the attic </s>
<s> The old simpleton </s>
<s> it is as dark as a tomb up there </s>
<s> But she does not know anything about art, and so she has no reverence for it </s>
<s> When I showed her my "Map of the Fortifications of Paris," she said it was rubbish </s>
<s> Well, from nursing those portraits so long, I have come at last to have a perfect infatuation for art </s>
<s> I have a teacher now, and my enthusiasm continually and tumultuously grows, as I learn to use with more and more facility the pencil, brush, and graver </s>
<s> I am studying under De Mellville, the house and portrait painter </s>
<s> (His name was Smith when he lived in the West.) He does any kind of artist work a body wants, having a genius that is universal, like Michael Angelo </s>
<s> Resembles that great artist, in fact </s>
<s> The back of his head is like this, and he wears his hat-brim tilted down on his nose to expose it </s>
<s> I have been studying under De Mellville several months now </s>
<s> The first month I painted fences, and gave general satisfaction </s>
<s> The next month I white-washed a barn </s>
<s> The third, I was doing tin roofs; the forth, common signs; the fifth, statuary to stand before cigar shops </s>
<s> This present month is only the sixth, and I am already in portraits </s>
<s> The humble offering which accompanies these remarks (see figure)--the portrait of his Majesty William III., King of Prussia--is my fifth attempt in portraits, and my greatest success </s>
<s> It has received unbounded praise from all classes of the community, but that which gratifies me most is the frequent and cordial verdict that it resembles the GALAXY portraits </s>
<s> Those were my first love, my earliest admiration, the original source and incentive of my art-ambition </s>
<s> Whatever I am in Art today, I owe to these portraits </s>
<s> I ask no credit for myself--I deserve none </s>
<s> And I never take any, either </s>
<s> Many a stranger has come to my exhibition (for I have had my portrait of King William on exhibition at one dollar a ticket), and would have gone away blessing ME, if I had let him, but I never did </s>
<s> I always stated where I got the idea </s>
<s> King William wears large bushy side-whiskers, and some critics have thought that this portrait would be more complete if they were added </s>
<s> But it was not possible </s>
<s> There was not room for side-whiskers and epaulets both, and so I let the whiskers go, and put in the epaulets, for the sake of style </s>
<s> That thing on his hat is an eagle </s>
<s> The Prussian eagle--it is a national emblem </s>
<s> When I say hat I mean helmet; but it seems impossible to make a picture of a helmet that a body can have confidence in </s>
<s> I wish kind friends everywhere would aid me in my endeavor to attract a little attention to the GALAXY portraits </s>
<s> I feel persuaded it can be accomplished, if the course to be pursued be chosen with judgment </s>
<s> I write for that magazine all the time, and so do many abler men, and if I can get these portraits into universal favor, it is all I ask; the reading-matter will take care of itself </s>

<s> DOES THE RACE OF MAN LOVE A LORD </s>
<s> Often a quite assified remark becomes sanctified by use and petrified by custom; it is then a permanency, its term of activity a geologic period </s>
<s> The day after the arrival of Prince Henry I met an English friend, and he rubbed his hands and broke out with a remark that was charged to the brim with joy--joy that was evidently a pleasant salve to an old sore place: "Many a time I've had to listen without retort to an old saying that is irritatingly true, and until now seemed to offer no chance for a return jibe: 'An Englishman does dearly love a lord'; but after this I shall talk back, and say, 'How about the Americans'?" It is a curious thing, the currency that an idiotic saying can get </s>
<s> The man that first says it thinks he has made a discovery </s>
<s> The man he says it to, thinks the same </s>
<s> It departs on its travels, is received everywhere with admiring acceptance, and not only as a piece of rare and acute observation, but as being exhaustively true and profoundly wise; and so it presently takes its place in the world's list of recognized and established wisdoms, and after that no one thinks of examining it to see whether it is really entitled to its high honors or not </s>
<s> I call to mind instances of this in two well-established proverbs, whose dullness is not surpassed by the one about the Englishman and his love for a lord: one of them records the American's Adoration of the Almighty Dollar, the other the American millionaire-girl's ambition to trade cash for a title, with a husband thrown in </s>
<s> It isn't merely the American that adores the Almighty Dollar, it is the human race </s>
<s> The human race has always adored the hatful of shells, or the bale of calico, or the half-bushel of brass rings, or the handful of steel fish-hooks, or the houseful of black wives, or the zareba full of cattle, or the two-score camels and asses, or the factory, or the farm, or the block of buildings, or the railroad bonds, or the bank stock, or the hoarded cash, or--anything that stands for wealth and consideration and independence, and can secure to the possessor that most precious of all things, another man's envy </s>
<s> It was a dull person that invented the idea that the American's devotion to the dollar is more strenuous than another's </s>
<s> Rich American girls do buy titles, but they did not invent that idea; it had been worn threadbare several hundred centuries before America was discovered </s>
<s> European girls still exploit it as briskly as ever; and, when a title is not to be had for the money in hand, they buy the husband without it </s>
<s> They must put up the "dot," or there is no trade </s>
<s> The commercialization of brides is substantially universal, except in America </s>
<s> It exists with us, to some little extent, but in no degree approaching a custom </s>
<s> "The Englishman dearly loves a lord" </s>
<s> What is the soul and source of this love </s>
<s> I think the thing could be more correctly worded: "The human race dearly envies a lord" </s>
<s> That is to say, it envies the lord's place </s>
<s> Why </s>
<s> On two accounts, I think: its Power and its Conspicuousness </s>
<s> Where Conspicuousness carries with it a Power which, by the light of our own observation and experience, we are able to measure and comprehend, I think our envy of the possessor is as deep and as passionate as is that of any other nation </s>
<s> No one can care less for a lord than the backwoodsman, who has had no personal contact with lords and has seldom heard them spoken of; but I will not allow that any Englishman has a profounder envy of a lord than has the average American who has lived long years in a European capital and fully learned how immense is the position the lord occupies </s>
<s> Of any ten thousand Americans who eagerly gather, at vast inconvenience, to get a glimpse of Prince Henry, all but a couple of hundred will be there out of an immense curiosity; they are burning up with desire to see a personage who is so much talked about </s>
<s> They envy him; but it is Conspicuousness they envy mainly, not the Power that is lodged in his royal quality and position, for they have but a vague and spectral knowledge and appreciation of that; though their environment and associations they have been accustomed to regard such things lightly, and as not being very real; consequently, they are not able to value them enough to consumingly envy them </s>
<s> But, whenever an American (or other human being) is in the presence, for the first time, of a combination of great Power and Conspicuousness which he thoroughly understands and appreciates, his eager curiosity and pleasure will be well-sodden with that other passion--envy--whether he suspects it or not </s>
<s> At any time, on any day, in any part of America, you can confer a happiness upon any passing stranger by calling his attention to any other passing stranger and saying: "Do you see that gentleman going along there </s>
<s> It is Mr Rockefeller" </s>
<s> Watch his eye </s>
<s> It is a combination of power and conspicuousness which the man understands </s>
<s> When we understand rank, we always like to rub against it </s>
<s> When a man is conspicuous, we always want to see him </s>
<s> Also, if he will pay us an attention we will manage to remember it </s>
<s> Also, we will mention it now and then, casually; sometimes to a friend, or if a friend is not handy, we will make out with a stranger </s>
<s> Well, then, what is rank, and what is conspicuousness </s>
<s> At once we think of kings and aristocracies, and of world-wide celebrities in soldierships, the arts, letters, etc, and we stop there </s>
<s> But that is a mistake </s>
<s> Rank holds its court and receives its homage on every round of the ladder, from the emperor down to the rat-catcher; and distinction, also, exists on every round of the ladder, and commands its due of deference and envy </s>
<s> To worship rank and distinction is the dear and valued privilege of all the human race, and it is freely and joyfully exercised in democracies as well as in monarchies--and even, to some extent, among those creatures whom we impertinently call the Lower Animals </s>
<s> For even they have some poor little vanities and foibles, though in this matter they are paupers as compared to us </s>
<s> A Chinese Emperor has the worship of his four hundred millions of subjects, but the rest of the world is indifferent to him </s>
<s> A Christian Emperor has the worship of his subjects and of a large part of the Christian world outside of his domains; but he is a matter of indifference to all China </s>
<s> A king, class A, has an extensive worship; a king, class B, has a less extensive worship; class C, class D, class E get a steadily diminishing share of worship; class L (Sultan of Zanzibar), class P (Sultan of Sulu), and class W (half-king of Samoa), get no worship at all outside their own little patch of sovereignty </s>
<s> Take the distinguished people along down </s>
<s> Each has his group of homage-payers </s>
<s> In the navy, there are many groups; they start with the Secretary and the Admiral, and go down to the quartermaster--and below; for there will be groups among the sailors, and each of these groups will have a tar who is distinguished for his battles, or his strength, or his daring, or his profanity, and is admired and envied by his group </s>
<s> The same with the army; the same with the literary and journalistic craft; the publishing craft; the cod-fishery craft; Standard Oil; U </s>
<s> S </s>
<s> Steel; the class A hotel--and the rest of the alphabet in that line; the class A prize-fighter--and the rest of the alphabet in his line--clear down to the lowest and obscurest six-boy gang of little gamins, with its one boy that can thrash the rest, and to whom he is king of Samoa, bottom of the royal race, but looked up to with a most ardent admiration and envy </s>
<s> There is something pathetic, and funny, and pretty, about this human race's fondness for contact with power and distinction, and for the reflected glory it gets out of it </s>
<s> The king, class A, is happy in the state banquet and the military show which the emperor provides for him, and he goes home and gathers the queen and the princelings around him in the privacy of the spare room, and tells them all about it, and says: "His Imperial Majesty put his hand upon my shoulder in the most friendly way--just as friendly and familiar, oh, you can't imagine it!--and everybody SEEING him do it; charming, perfectly charming" </s>
<s> The king, class G, is happy in the cold collation and the police parade provided for him by the king, class B, and goes home and tells the family all about it, and says: "And His Majesty took me into his own private cabinet for a smoke and a chat, and there we sat just as sociable, and talking away and laughing and chatting, just the same as if we had been born in the same bunk; and all the servants in the anteroom could see us doing it </s>
<s> Oh, it was too lovely for anything" </s>
<s> The king, class Q, is happy in the modest entertainment furnished him by the king, class M, and goes home and tells the household about it, and is as grateful and joyful over it as were his predecessors in the gaudier attentions that had fallen to their larger lot </s>
<s> Emperors, kings, artisans, peasants, big people, little people--at the bottom we are all alike and all the same; all just alike on the inside, and when our clothes are off, nobody can tell which of us is which </s>
<s> We are unanimous in the pride we take in good and genuine compliments paid us, and distinctions conferred upon us, in attentions shown </s>
<s> There is not one of us, from the emperor down, but is made like that </s>
<s> Do I mean attentions shown us by the guest </s>
<s> No, I mean simply flattering attentions, let them come whence they may </s>
<s> We despise no source that can pay us a pleasing attention--there is no source that is humble enough for that </s>
<s> You have heard a dear little girl say to a frowzy and disreputable dog: "He came right to me and let me pat him on the head, and he wouldn't let the others touch him" </s>
<s> and you have seen her eyes dance with pride in that high distinction </s>
<s> You have often seen that </s>
<s> If the child were a princess, would that random dog be able to confer the like glory upon her with his pretty compliment </s>
<s> Yes; and even in her mature life and seated upon a throne, she would still remember it, still recall it, still speak of it with frank satisfaction </s>
<s> That charming and lovable German princess and poet, Carmen Sylva, Queen of Roumania, remembers yet that the flowers of the woods and fields "talked to her" when she was a girl, and she sets it down in her latest book; and that the squirrels conferred upon her and her father the valued compliment of not being afraid of them; and "once one of them, holding a nut between its sharp little teeth, ran right up against my father"--it has the very note of "He came right to me and let me pat him on the head"--"and when it saw itself reflected in his boot it was very much surprised, and stopped for a long time to contemplate itself in the polished leather"--then it went its way </s>
<s> And the birds </s>
<s> she still remembers with pride that "they came boldly into my room," when she had neglected her "duty" and put no food on the window-sill for them; she knew all the wild birds, and forgets the royal crown on her head to remember with pride that they knew her; also that the wasp and the bee were personal friends of hers, and never forgot that gracious relationship to her injury: "never have I been stung by a wasp or a bee" </s>
<s> And here is that proud note again that sings in that little child's elation in being singled out, among all the company of children, for the random dog's honor-conferring attentions </s>
<s> "Even in the very worst summer for wasps, when, in lunching out of doors, our table was covered with them and every one else was stung, they never hurt me" </s>
<s> When a queen whose qualities of mind and heart and character are able to add distinction to so distinguished a place as a throne, remembers with grateful exultation, after thirty years, honors and distinctions conferred upon her by the humble, wild creatures of the forest, we are helped to realize that complimentary attentions, homage, distinctions, are of no caste, but are above all cast--that they are a nobility-conferring power apart </s>
<s> We all like these things </s>
<s> When the gate-guard at the railway-station passes me through unchallenged and examines other people's tickets, I feel as the king, class A, felt when the emperor put the imperial hand on his shoulder, "everybody seeing him do it"; and as the child felt when the random dog allowed her to pat his head and ostracized the others; and as the princess felt when the wasps spared her and stung the rest; and I felt just so, four years ago in Vienna (and remember it yet), when the helmeted police shut me off, with fifty others, from a street which the Emperor was to pass through, and the captain of the squad turned and saw the situation and said indignantly to that guard: "Can't you see it is the Herr Mark Twain </s>
<s> Let him through" </s>
<s> It was four years ago; but it will be four hundred before I forget the wind of self-complacency that rose in me, and strained my buttons when I marked the deference for me evoked in the faces of my fellow-rabble, and noted, mingled with it, a puzzled and resentful expression which said, as plainly as speech could have worded it: "And who in the nation is the Herr Mark Twain UM GOTTESWILLEN" </s>
<s> How many times in your life have you heard this boastful remark: "I stood as close to him as I am to you; I could have put out my hand and touched him" </s>
<s> We have all heard it many and many a time </s>
<s> It was a proud distinction to be able to say those words </s>
<s> It brought envy to the speaker, a kind of glory; and he basked in it and was happy through all his veins </s>
<s> And who was it he stood so close to </s>
<s> The answer would cover all the grades </s>
<s> Sometimes it was a king; sometimes it was a renowned highwayman; sometimes it was an unknown man killed in an extraordinary way and made suddenly famous by it; always it was a person who was for the moment the subject of public interest of a village </s>
<s> "I was there, and I saw it myself" </s>
<s> That is a common and envy-compelling remark </s>
<s> It can refer to a battle; to a handing; to a coronation; to the killing of Jumbo by the railway-train; to the arrival of Jenny Lind at the Battery; to the meeting of the President and Prince Henry; to the chase of a murderous maniac; to the disaster in the tunnel; to the explosion in the subway; to a remarkable dog-fight; to a village church struck by lightning </s>
<s> It will be said, more or less causally, by everybody in America who has seen Prince Henry do anything, or try to </s>
<s> The man who was absent and didn't see him to anything, will scoff </s>
<s> It is his privilege; and he can make capital out of it, too; he will seem, even to himself, to be different from other Americans, and better </s>
<s> As his opinion of his superior Americanism grows, and swells, and concentrates and coagulates, he will go further and try to belittle the distinction of those that saw the Prince do things, and will spoil their pleasure in it if he can </s>
<s> My life has been embittered by that kind of person </s>
<s> If you are able to tell of a special distinction that has fallen to your lot, it gravels them; they cannot bear it; and they try to make believe that the thing you took for a special distinction was nothing of the kind and was meant in quite another way </s>
<s> Once I was received in private audience by an emperor </s>
<s> Last week I was telling a jealous person about it, and I could see him wince under it, see him bite, see him suffer </s>
<s> I revealed the whole episode to him with considerable elaboration and nice attention to detail </s>

<s> "An Englishman (or other human being) does dearly love a lord," (or other conspicuous person.) It includes us all </s>
<s> We love to be noticed by the conspicuous person; we love to be associated with such, or with a conspicuous event, even in a seventh-rate fashion, even in the forty-seventh, if we cannot do better </s>
<s> This accounts for some of our curious tastes in mementos </s>
<s> It accounts for the large private trade in the Prince of Wales's hair, which chambermaids were able to drive in that article of commerce when the Prince made the tour of the world in the long ago--hair which probably did not always come from his brush, since enough of it was marketed to refurnish a bald comet; it accounts for the fact that the rope which lynches a negro in the presence of ten thousand Christian spectators is salable five minutes later at two dollars and inch; it accounts for the mournful fact that a royal personage does not venture to wear buttons on his coat in public </s>
<s> We do love a lord--and by that term I mean any person whose situation is higher than our own </s>
<s> The lord of the group, for instance: a group of peers, a group of millionaires, a group of hoodlums, a group of sailors, a group of newsboys, a group of saloon politicians, a group of college girls </s>
<s> No royal person has ever been the object of a more delirious loyalty and slavish adoration than is paid by the vast Tammany herd to its squalid idol in Wantage </s>
<s> There is not a bifurcated animal in that menagerie that would not be proud to appear in a newspaper picture in his company </s>
<s> At the same time, there are some in that organization who would scoff at the people who have been daily pictured in company with Prince Henry, and would say vigorously that THEY would not consent to be photographed with him--a statement which would not be true in any instance </s>
<s> There are hundreds of people in America who would frankly say to you that they would not be proud to be photographed in a group with the Prince, if invited; and some of these unthinking people would believe it when they said it; yet in no instance would it be true </s>
<s> We have a large population, but we have not a large enough one, by several millions, to furnish that man </s>
<s> He has not yet been begotten, and in fact he is not begettable </s>
<s> You may take any of the printed groups, and there isn't a person in the dim background who isn't visibly trying to be vivid; if it is a crowd of ten thousand--ten thousand proud, untamed democrats, horny-handed sons of toil and of politics, and fliers of the eagle--there isn't one who is trying to keep out of range, there isn't one who isn't plainly meditating a purchase of the paper in the morning, with the intention of hunting himself out in the picture and of framing and keeping it if he shall find so much of his person in it as his starboard ear </s>
<s> We all love to get some of the drippings of Conspicuousness, and we will put up with a single, humble drip, if we can't get any more </s>
<s> We may pretend otherwise, in conversation; but we can't pretend it to ourselves privately--and we don't </s>
<s> We do confess in public that we are the noblest work of God, being moved to it by long habit, and teaching, and superstition; but deep down in the secret places of our souls we recognize that, if we ARE the noblest work, the less said about it the better </s>
<s> We of the North poke fun at the South for its fondness of titles--a fondness for titles pure and simple, regardless of whether they are genuine or pinchbeck </s>
<s> We forget that whatever a Southerner likes the rest of the human race likes, and that there is no law of predilection lodged in one people that is absent from another people </s>

<s> We can soon acquire that Southern disease if some one will give it a start </s>
<s> It already has a start, in fact </s>
<s> I have been personally acquainted with over eighty-four thousand persons who, at one time or another in their lives, have served for a year or two on the staffs of our multitudinous governors, and through that fatality have been generals temporarily, and colonels temporarily, and judge-advocates temporarily; but I have known only nine among them who could be hired to let the title go when it ceased to be legitimate </s>
<s> I know thousands and thousands of governors who ceased to be governors away back in the last century; but I am acquainted with only three who would answer your letter if you failed to call them "Governor" in it </s>
<s> I know acres and acres of men who have done time in a legislature in prehistoric days, but among them is not half an acre whose resentment you would not raise if you addressed them as "Mr" instead of "Hon" </s>
<s> The first thing a legislature does is to convene in an impressive legislative attitude, and get itself photographed </s>
<s> Each member frames his copy and takes it to the woods and hangs it up in the most aggressively conspicuous place in his house; and if you visit the house and fail to inquire what that accumulation is, the conversation will be brought around to it by that aforetime legislator, and he will show you a figure in it which in the course of years he has almost obliterated with the smut of his finger-marks, and say with a solemn joy, "It's me" </s>
<s> Have you ever seen a country Congressman enter the hotel breakfast-room in Washington with his letters?--and sit at his table and let on to read them?--and wrinkle his brows and frown statesman-like?--keeping a furtive watch-out over his glasses all the while to see if he is being observed and admired?--those same old letters which he fetches in every morning </s>
<s> Have you seen it </s>
<s> Have you seen him show off </s>
<s> It is THE sight of the national capital </s>
<s> Except one; a pathetic one </s>
<s> That is the ex-Congressman: the poor fellow whose life has been ruined by a two-year taste of glory and of fictitious consequence; who has been superseded, and ought to take his heartbreak home and hide it, but cannot tear himself away from the scene of his lost little grandeur; and so he lingers, and still lingers, year after year, unconsidered, sometimes snubbed, ashamed of his fallen estate, and valiantly trying to look otherwise; dreary and depressed, but counterfeiting breeziness and gaiety, hailing with chummy familiarity, which is not always welcomed, the more-fortunes who are still in place and were once his mates </s>
<s> Have you seen him </s>
<s> He clings piteously to the one little shred that is left of his departed distinction--the "privilege of the floor"; and works it hard and gets what he can out of it </s>
<s> That is the saddest figure I know of </s>
<s> Yes, we do so love our little distinctions </s>
<s> And then we loftily scoff at a Prince for enjoying his larger ones; forgetting that if we only had his chance--ah </s>
<s> "Senator" is not a legitimate title </s>
<s> A Senator has no more right to be addressed by it than have you or I; but, in the several state capitals and in Washington, there are five thousand Senators who take very kindly to that fiction, and who purr gratefully when you call them by it--which you may do quite unrebuked </s>
<s> Then those same Senators smile at the self-constructed majors and generals and judges of the South </s>
<s> Indeed, we do love our distinctions, get them how we may </s>
<s> And we work them for all they are worth </s>

<s> As a race, we do certainly love a lord--let him be Croker, or a duke, or a prize-fighter, or whatever other personage shall chance to be the head of our group </s>
<s> Many years ago, I saw a greasy youth in overalls standing by the HERALD office, with an expectant look in his face </s>
<s> Soon a large man passed out, and gave him a pat on the shoulder </s>
<s> That was what the boy was waiting for--the large man's notice </s>
<s> The pat made him proud and happy, and the exultation inside of him shone out through his eyes; and his mates were there to see the pat and envy it and wish they could have that glory </s>
<s> The boy belonged down cellar in the press-room, the large man was king of the upper floors, foreman of the composing-room </s>
<s> The light in the boy's face was worship, the foreman was his lord, head of his group </s>
<s> The pat was an accolade </s>

<s> EXTRACTS FROM ADAM'S DIARY MONDAY.--This new creature with the long hair is a good deal in the way </s>
<s> It is always hanging around and following me about </s>
<s> I don't like this; I am not used to company </s>
<s> I wish it would stay with the other animals... </s>
<s> Cloudy today, wind in the east; think we shall have rain... </s>
<s> WE </s>
<s> Where did I get that word--the new creature uses it </s>
<s> TUESDAY.--Been examining the great waterfall </s>
<s> It is the finest thing on the estate, I think </s>
<s> The new creature calls it Niagara Falls--why, I am sure I do not know </s>
<s> Says it LOOKS like Niagara Falls </s>
<s> That is not a reason, it is mere waywardness and imbecility </s>
<s> I get no chance to name anything myself </s>
<s> The new creature names everything that comes along, before I can get in a protest </s>
<s> And always that same pretext is offered--it LOOKS like the thing </s>
<s> There is a dodo, for instance </s>
<s> Says the moment one looks at it one sees at a glance that it "looks like a dodo" </s>
<s> It will have to keep that name, no doubt </s>
<s> It wearies me to fret about it, and it does no good, anyway </s>
<s> Dodo </s>
<s> It looks no more like a dodo than I do </s>
<s> WEDNESDAY.--Built me a shelter against the rain, but could not have it to myself in peace </s>
<s> The new creature intruded </s>
<s> When I tried to put it out it shed water out of the holes it looks with, and wiped it away with the back of its paws, and made a noise such as some of the other animals make when they are in distress </s>
<s> I wish it would not talk; it is always talking </s>
<s> That sounds like a cheap fling at the poor creature, a slur; but I do not mean it so </s>
<s> I have never heard the human voice before, and any new and strange sound intruding itself here upon the solemn hush of these dreaming solitudes offends my ear and seems a false note </s>
<s> And this new sound is so close to me; it is right at my shoulder, right at my ear, first on one side and then on the other, and I am used only to sounds that are more or less distant from me </s>
<s> FRIDAY </s>
<s> The naming goes recklessly on, in spite of anything I can do </s>
<s> I had a very good name for the estate, and it was musical and pretty--GARDEN OF EDEN </s>
<s> Privately, I continue to call it that, but not any longer publicly </s>
<s> The new creature says it is all woods and rocks and scenery, and therefore has no resemblance to a garden </s>
<s> Says it LOOKS like a park, and does not look like anything BUT a park </s>
<s> Consequently, without consulting me, it has been new-named NIAGARA FALLS PARK </s>
<s> This is sufficiently high-handed, it seems to me </s>
<s> And already there is a sign up: KEEP OFF THE GRASS My life is not as happy as it was </s>
<s> SATURDAY.--The new creature eats too much fruit </s>
<s> We are going to run short, most likely </s>
<s> "We" again--that is ITS word; mine, too, now, from hearing it so much </s>
<s> Good deal of fog this morning </s>
<s> I do not go out in the fog myself </s>
<s> This new creature does </s>
<s> It goes out in all weathers, and stumps right in with its muddy feet </s>
<s> And talks </s>
<s> It used to be so pleasant and quiet here </s>
<s> SUNDAY.--Pulled through </s>
<s> This day is getting to be more and more trying </s>
<s> It was selected and set apart last November as a day of rest </s>
<s> I had already six of them per week before </s>
<s> This morning found the new creature trying to clod apples out of that forbidden tree </s>
<s> MONDAY.--The new creature says its name is Eve </s>
<s> That is all right, I have no objections </s>
<s> Says it is to call it by, when I want it to come </s>
<s> I said it was superfluous, then </s>
<s> The word evidently raised me in its respect; and indeed it is a large, good word and will bear repetition </s>
<s> It says it is not an It, it is a She </s>
<s> This is probably doubtful; yet it is all one to me; what she is were nothing to me if she would but go by herself and not talk </s>
<s> TUESDAY.--She has littered the whole estate with execrable names and offensive signs: This way to the Whirlpool This way to Goat Island Cave of the Winds this way She says this park would make a tidy summer resort if there was any custom for it </s>
<s> Summer resort--another invention of hers--just words, without any meaning </s>
<s> What is a summer resort </s>
<s> But it is best not to ask her, she has such a rage for explaining </s>
<s> FRIDAY.--She has taken to beseeching me to stop going over the Falls </s>
<s> What harm does it do </s>
<s> Says it makes her shudder </s>
<s> I wonder why; I have always done it--always liked the plunge, and coolness </s>
<s> I supposed it was what the Falls were for </s>
<s> They have no other use that I can see, and they must have been made for something </s>
<s> She says they were only made for scenery--like the rhinoceros and the mastodon </s>
<s> I went over the Falls in a barrel--not satisfactory to her </s>
<s> Went over in a tub--still not satisfactory </s>
<s> Swam the Whirlpool and the Rapids in a fig-leaf suit </s>
<s> It got much damaged </s>
<s> Hence, tedious complaints about my extravagance </s>
<s> I am too much hampered here </s>
<s> What I need is a change of scene </s>
<s> SATURDAY.--I escaped last Tuesday night, and traveled two days, and built me another shelter in a secluded place, and obliterated my tracks as well as I could, but she hunted me out by means of a beast which she has tamed and calls a wolf, and came making that pitiful noise again, and shedding that water out of the places she looks with </s>
<s> I was obliged to return with her, but will presently emigrate again when occasion offers </s>
<s> She engages herself in many foolish things; among others; to study out why the animals called lions and tigers live on grass and flowers, when, as she says, the sort of teeth they wear would indicate that they were intended to eat each other </s>
<s> This is foolish, because to do that would be to kill each other, and that would introduce what, as I understand, is called "death"; and death, as I have been told, has not yet entered the Park </s>
<s> Which is a pity, on some accounts </s>
<s> SUNDAY.--Pulled through </s>
<s> MONDAY.--I believe I see what the week is for: it is to give time to rest up from the weariness of Sunday </s>
<s> It seems a good idea </s>
<s> .. </s>
<s> She has been climbing that tree again </s>
<s> Clodded her out of it </s>
<s> She said nobody was looking </s>
<s> Seems to consider that a sufficient justification for chancing any dangerous thing </s>
<s> Told her that </s>
<s> The word justification moved her admiration--and envy, too, I thought </s>
<s> It is a good word </s>
<s> TUESDAY.--She told me she was made out of a rib taken from my body </s>
<s> This is at least doubtful, if not more than that </s>
<s> I have not missed any rib... </s>
<s> She is in much trouble about the buzzard; says grass does not agree with it; is afraid she can't raise it; thinks it was intended to live on decayed flesh </s>
<s> The buzzard must get along the best it can with what is provided </s>
<s> We cannot overturn the whole scheme to accommodate the buzzard </s>
<s> SATURDAY.--She fell in the pond yesterday when she was looking at herself in it, which she is always doing </s>
<s> She nearly strangled, and said it was most uncomfortable </s>
<s> This made her sorry for the creatures which live in there, which she calls fish, for she continues to fasten names on to things that don't need them and don't come when they are called by them, which is a matter of no consequence to her, she is such a numbskull, anyway; so she got a lot of them out and brought them in last night and put them in my bed to keep warm, but I have noticed them now and then all day and I don't see that they are any happier there then they were before, only quieter </s>
<s> When night comes I shall throw them outdoors </s>
<s> I will not sleep with them again, for I find them clammy and unpleasant to lie among when a person hasn't anything on </s>
<s> SUNDAY.--Pulled through </s>
<s> TUESDAY.--She has taken up with a snake now </s>
<s> The other animals are glad, for she was always experimenting with them and bothering them; and I am glad because the snake talks, and this enables me to get a rest </s>
<s> FRIDAY.--She says the snake advises her to try the fruit of the tree, and says the result will be a great and fine and noble education </s>
<s> I told her there would be another result, too--it would introduce death into the world </s>
<s> That was a mistake--it had been better to keep the remark to myself; it only gave her an idea--she could save the sick buzzard, and furnish fresh meat to the despondent lions and tigers </s>
<s> I advised her to keep away from the tree </s>
<s> She said she wouldn't </s>
<s> I foresee trouble </s>
<s> Will emigrate </s>
<s> WEDNESDAY.--I have had a variegated time </s>
<s> I escaped last night, and rode a horse all night as fast as he could go, hoping to get clear of the Park and hide in some other country before the trouble should begin; but it was not to be </s>
<s> About an hour after sun-up, as I was riding through a flowery plain where thousands of animals were grazing, slumbering, or playing with each other, according to their wont, all of a sudden they broke into a tempest of frightful noises, and in one moment the plain was a frantic commotion and every beast was destroying its neighbor </s>
<s> I knew what it meant--Eve had eaten that fruit, and death was come into the world </s>
<s> .. </s>
<s> The tigers ate my house, paying no attention when I ordered them to desist, and they would have eaten me if I had stayed--which I didn't, but went away in much haste... </s>
<s> I found this place, outside the Park, and was fairly comfortable for a few days, but she has found me out </s>
<s> Found me out, and has named the place Tonawanda--says it LOOKS like that </s>
<s> In fact I was not sorry she came, for there are but meager pickings here, and she brought some of those apples </s>
<s> I was obliged to eat them, I was so hungry </s>
<s> It was against my principles, but I find that principles have no real force except when one is well fed... </s>
<s> She came curtained in boughs and bunches of leaves, and when I asked her what she meant by such nonsense, and snatched them away and threw them down, she tittered and blushed </s>
<s> I had never seen a person titter and blush before, and to me it seemed unbecoming and idiotic </s>
<s> She said I would soon know how it was myself </s>
<s> This was correct </s>
<s> Hungry as I was, I laid down the apple half-eaten--certainly the best one I ever saw, considering the lateness of the season--and arrayed myself in the discarded boughs and branches, and then spoke to her with some severity and ordered her to go and get some more and not make a spectacle or herself </s>
<s> She did it, and after this we crept down to where the wild-beast battle had been, and collected some skins, and I made her patch together a couple of suits proper for public occasions </s>

<s> She will be useful </s>
<s> I will superintend </s>
<s> TEN DAYS LATER.--She accuses ME of being the cause of our disaster </s>
<s> She says, with apparent sincerity and truth, that the Serpent assured her that the forbidden fruit was not apples, it was chestnuts </s>
<s> I said I was innocent, then, for I had not eaten any chestnuts </s>
<s> She said the Serpent informed her that "chestnut" was a figurative term meaning an aged and moldy joke </s>
<s> I turned pale at that, for I have made many jokes to pass the weary time, and some of them could have been of that sort, though I had honestly supposed that they were new when I made them </s>
<s> She asked me if I had made one just at the time of the catastrophe </s>
<s> I was obliged to admit that I had made one to myself, though not aloud </s>
<s> It was this </s>
<s> I was thinking about the Falls, and I said to myself, "How wonderful it is to see that vast body of water tumble down there" </s>
<s> Then in an instant a bright thought flashed into my head, and I let it fly, saying, "It would be a deal more wonderful to see it tumble UP there"!--and I was just about to kill myself with laughing at it when all nature broke loose in war and death and I had to flee for my life </s>
<s> "There," she said, with triumph, "that is just it; the Serpent mentioned that very jest, and called it the First Chestnut, and said it was coeval with the creation" </s>
<s> Alas, I am indeed to blame </s>
<s> Would that I were not witty; oh, that I had never had that radiant thought </s>
<s> NEXT YEAR.--We have named it Cain </s>
<s> She caught it while I was up country trapping on the North Shore of the Erie; caught it in the timber a couple of miles from our dug-out--or it might have been four, she isn't certain which </s>
<s> It resembles us in some ways, and may be a relation </s>
<s> That is what she thinks, but this is an error, in my judgment </s>
<s> The difference in size warrants the conclusion that it is a different and new kind of animal--a fish, perhaps, though when I put it in the water to see, it sank, and she plunged in and snatched it out before there was opportunity for the experiment to determine the matter </s>
<s> I still think it is a fish, but she is indifferent about what it is, and will not let me have it to try </s>
<s> I do not understand this </s>
<s> The coming of the creature seems to have changed her whole nature and made her unreasonable about experiments </s>
<s> She thinks more of it than she does of any of the other animals, but is not able to explain why </s>
<s> Her mind is disordered--everything shows it </s>
<s> Sometimes she carries the fish in her arms half the night when it complains and wants to get to the water </s>
<s> At such times the water comes out of the places in her face that she looks out of, and she pats the fish on the back and makes soft sounds with her mouth to soothe it, and betrays sorrow and solicitude in a hundred ways </s>
<s> I have never seen her do like this with any other fish, and it troubles me greatly </s>
<s> She used to carry the young tigers around so, and play with them, before we lost our property, but it was only play; she never took on about them like this when their dinner disagreed with them </s>
<s> SUNDAY.--She doesn't work, Sundays, but lies around all tired out, and likes to have the fish wallow over her; and she makes fool noises to amuse it, and pretends to chew its paws, and that makes it laugh </s>
<s> I have not seen a fish before that could laugh </s>
<s> This makes me doubt... </s>
<s> I have come to like Sunday myself </s>
<s> Superintending all the week tires a body so </s>
<s> There ought to be more Sundays </s>
<s> In the old days they were tough, but now they come handy </s>
<s> WEDNESDAY.--It isn't a fish </s>
<s> I cannot quite make out what it is </s>
<s> It makes curious devilish noises when not satisfied, and says "goo-goo" when it is </s>
<s> It is not one of us, for it doesn't walk; it is not a bird, for it doesn't fly; it is not a frog, for it doesn't hop; it is not a snake, for it doesn't crawl; I feel sure it is not a fish, though I cannot get a chance to find out whether it can swim or not </s>
<s> It merely lies around, and mostly on its back, with its feet up </s>
<s> I have not seen any other animal do that before </s>
<s> I said I believed it was an enigma; but she only admired the word without understanding it </s>
<s> In my judgment it is either an enigma or some kind of a bug </s>
<s> If it dies, I will take it apart and see what its arrangements are </s>
<s> I never had a thing perplex me so </s>
<s> THREE MONTHS LATER.--The perplexity augments instead of diminishing </s>
<s> I sleep but little </s>
<s> It has ceased from lying around, and goes about on its four legs now </s>
<s> Yet it differs from the other four legged animals, in that its front legs are unusually short, consequently this causes the main part of its person to stick up uncomfortably high in the air, and this is not attractive </s>
<s> It is built much as we are, but its method of traveling shows that it is not of our breed </s>
<s> The short front legs and long hind ones indicate that it is a of the kangaroo family, but it is a marked variation of that species, since the true kangaroo hops, whereas this one never does </s>
<s> Still it is a curious and interesting variety, and has not been catalogued before </s>
<s> As I discovered it, I have felt justified in securing the credit of the discovery by attaching my name to it, and hence have called it KANGAROORUM ADAMIENSIS... </s>
<s> It must have been a young one when it came, for it has grown exceedingly since </s>
<s> It must be five times as big, now, as it was then, and when discontented it is able to make from twenty-two to thirty-eight times the noise it made at first </s>
<s> Coercion does not modify this, but has the contrary effect </s>
<s> For this reason I discontinued the system </s>
<s> She reconciles it by persuasion, and by giving it things which she had previously told me she wouldn't give it </s>
<s> As already observed, I was not at home when it first came, and she told me she found it in the woods </s>
<s> It seems odd that it should be the only one, yet it must be so, for I have worn myself out these many weeks trying to find another one to add to my collection, and for this to play with; for surely then it would be quieter and we could tame it more easily </s>
<s> But I find none, nor any vestige of any; and strangest of all, no tracks </s>
<s> It has to live on the ground, it cannot help itself; therefore, how does it get about without leaving a track </s>
<s> I have set a dozen traps, but they do no good </s>
<s> I catch all small animals except that one; animals that merely go into the trap out of curiosity, I think, to see what the milk is there for </s>
<s> They never drink it </s>
<s> THREE MONTHS LATER.--The Kangaroo still continues to grow, which is very strange and perplexing </s>
<s> I never knew one to be so long getting its growth </s>
<s> It has fur on its head now; not like kangaroo fur, but exactly like our hair except that it is much finer and softer, and instead of being black is red </s>
<s> I am like to lose my mind over the capricious and harassing developments of this unclassifiable zoological freak </s>
<s> If I could catch another one--but that is hopeless; it is a new variety, and the only sample; this is plain </s>
<s> But I caught a true kangaroo and brought it in, thinking that this one, being lonesome, would rather have that for company than have no kin at all, or any animal it could feel a nearness to or get sympathy from in its forlorn condition here among strangers who do not know its ways or habits, or what to do to make it feel that it is among friends; but it was a mistake--it went into such fits at the sight of the kangaroo that I was convinced it had never seen one before </s>
<s> I pity the poor noisy little animal, but there is nothing I can do to make it happy </s>
<s> If I could tame it--but that is out of the question; the more I try the worse I seem to make it </s>
<s> It grieves me to the heart to see it in its little storms of sorrow and passion </s>
<s> I wanted to let it go, but she wouldn't hear of it </s>
<s> That seemed cruel and not like her; and yet she may be right </s>
<s> It might be lonelier than ever; for since I cannot find another one, how could IT </s>
<s> FIVE MONTHS LATER.--It is not a kangaroo </s>
<s> No, for it supports itself by holding to her finger, and thus goes a few steps on its hind legs, and then falls down </s>
<s> It is probably some kind of a bear; and yet it has no tail--as yet--and no fur, except upon its head </s>
<s> It still keeps on growing--that is a curious circumstance, for bears get their growth earlier than this </s>
<s> Bears are dangerous--since our catastrophe--and I shall not be satisfied to have this one prowling about the place much longer without a muzzle on </s>
<s> I have offered to get her a kangaroo if she would let this one go, but it did no good--she is determined to run us into all sorts of foolish risks, I think </s>
<s> She was not like this before she lost her mind </s>
<s> A FORTNIGHT LATER.--I examined its mouth </s>
<s> There is no danger yet: it has only one tooth </s>
<s> It has no tail yet </s>
<s> It makes more noise now than it ever did before--and mainly at night </s>
<s> I have moved out </s>
<s> But I shall go over, mornings, to breakfast, and see if it has more teeth </s>
<s> If it gets a mouthful of teeth it will be time for it to go, tail or no tail, for a bear does not need a tail in order to be dangerous </s>
<s> FOUR MONTHS LATER.--I have been off hunting and fishing a month, up in the region that she calls Buffalo; I don't know why, unless it is because there are not any buffaloes there </s>
<s> Meantime the bear has learned to paddle around all by itself on its hind legs, and says "poppa" and "momma" </s>
<s> It is certainly a new species </s>
<s> This resemblance to words may be purely accidental, of course, and may have no purpose or meaning; but even in that case it is still extraordinary, and is a thing which no other bear can do </s>
<s> This imitation of speech, taken together with general absence of fur and entire absence of tail, sufficiently indicates that this is a new kind of bear </s>
<s> The further study of it will be exceedingly interesting </s>
<s> Meantime I will go off on a far expedition among the forests of the north and make an exhaustive search </s>
<s> There must certainly be another one somewhere, and this one will be less dangerous when it has company of its own species </s>
<s> I will go straightway; but I will muzzle this one first </s>
<s> THREE MONTHS LATER.--It has been a weary, weary hunt, yet I have had no success </s>
<s> In the mean time, without stirring from the home estate, she has caught another one </s>
<s> I never saw such luck </s>
<s> I might have hunted these woods a hundred years, I never would have run across that thing </s>
<s> NEXT DAY.--I have been comparing the new one with the old one, and it is perfectly plain that they are of the same breed </s>
<s> I was going to stuff one of them for my collection, but she is prejudiced against it for some reason or other; so I have relinquished the idea, though I think it is a mistake </s>
<s> It would be an irreparable loss to science if they should get away </s>
<s> The old one is tamer than it was and can laugh and talk like a parrot, having learned this, no doubt, from being with the parrot so much, and having the imitative faculty in a high developed degree </s>
<s> I shall be astonished if it turns out to be a new kind of parrot; and yet I ought not to be astonished, for it has already been everything else it could think of since those first days when it was a fish </s>
