<s> TEN YEARS LATER.--They are BOYS; we found it out long ago </s>
<s> It was their coming in that small immature shape that puzzled us; we were not used to it </s>
<s> There are some girls now </s>
<s> Abel is a good boy, but if Cain had stayed a bear it would have improved him </s>
<s> After all these years, I see that I was mistaken about Eve in the beginning; it is better to live outside the Garden with her than inside it without her </s>
<s> At first I thought she talked too much; but now I should be sorry to have that voice fall silent and pass out of my life </s>
<s> Blessed be the chestnut that brought us near together and taught me to know the goodness of her heart and the sweetness of her spirit </s>
<s> EVE'S DIARY Translated from the Original SATURDAY.--I am almost a whole day old, now </s>
<s> I arrived yesterday </s>
<s> That is as it seems to me </s>
<s> And it must be so, for if there was a day-before-yesterday I was not there when it happened, or I should remember it </s>
<s> It could be, of course, that it did happen, and that I was not noticing </s>
<s> Very well; I will be very watchful now, and if any day-before-yesterdays happen I will make a note of it </s>
<s> It will be best to start right and not let the record get confused, for some instinct tells me that these details are going to be important to the historian some day </s>
<s> For I feel like an experiment, I feel exactly like an experiment; it would be impossible for a person to feel more like an experiment than I do, and so I am coming to feel convinced that that is what I AM--an experiment; just an experiment, and nothing more </s>
<s> Then if I am an experiment, am I the whole of it </s>
<s> No, I think not; I think the rest of it is part of it </s>
<s> I am the main part of it, but I think the rest of it has its share in the matter </s>
<s> Is my position assured, or do I have to watch it and take care of it </s>
<s> The latter, perhaps </s>
<s> Some instinct tells me that eternal vigilance is the price of supremacy </s>
<s> (That is a good phrase, I think, for one so young.) Everything looks better today than it did yesterday </s>
<s> In the rush of finishing up yesterday, the mountains were left in a ragged condition, and some of the plains were so cluttered with rubbish and remnants that the aspects were quite distressing </s>
<s> Noble and beautiful works of art should not be subjected to haste; and this majestic new world is indeed a most noble and beautiful work </s>
<s> And certainly marvelously near to being perfect, notwithstanding the shortness of the time </s>
<s> There are too many stars in some places and not enough in others, but that can be remedied presently, no doubt </s>
<s> The moon got loose last night, and slid down and fell out of the scheme--a very great loss; it breaks my heart to think of it </s>
<s> There isn't another thing among the ornaments and decorations that is comparable to it for beauty and finish </s>
<s> It should have been fastened better </s>
<s> If we can only get it back again-- But of course there is no telling where it went to </s>
<s> And besides, whoever gets it will hide it; I know it because I would do it myself </s>
<s> I believe I can be honest in all other matters, but I already begin to realize that the core and center of my nature is love of the beautiful, a passion for the beautiful, and that it would not be safe to trust me with a moon that belonged to another person and that person didn't know I had it </s>
<s> I could give up a moon that I found in the daytime, because I should be afraid some one was looking; but if I found it in the dark, I am sure I should find some kind of an excuse for not saying anything about it </s>
<s> For I do love moons, they are so pretty and so romantic </s>
<s> I wish we had five or six; I would never go to bed; I should never get tired lying on the moss-bank and looking up at them </s>
<s> Stars are good, too </s>
<s> I wish I could get some to put in my hair </s>
<s> But I suppose I never can </s>
<s> You would be surprised to find how far off they are, for they do not look it </s>
<s> When they first showed, last night, I tried to knock some down with a pole, but it didn't reach, which astonished me; then I tried clods till I was all tired out, but I never got one </s>
<s> It was because I am left-handed and cannot throw good </s>
<s> Even when I aimed at the one I wasn't after I couldn't hit the other one, though I did make some close shots, for I saw the black blot of the clod sail right into the midst of the golden clusters forty or fifty times, just barely missing them, and if I could have held out a little longer maybe I could have got one </s>
<s> So I cried a little, which was natural, I suppose, for one of my age, and after I was rested I got a basket and started for a place on the extreme rim of the circle, where the stars were close to the ground and I could get them with my hands, which would be better, anyway, because I could gather them tenderly then, and not break them </s>
<s> But it was farther than I thought, and at last I had go give it up; I was so tired I couldn't drag my feet another step; and besides, they were sore and hurt me very much </s>
<s> I couldn't get back home; it was too far and turning cold; but I found some tigers and nestled in among them and was most adorably comfortable, and their breath was sweet and pleasant, because they live on strawberries </s>
<s> I had never seen a tiger before, but I knew them in a minute by the stripes </s>
<s> If I could have one of those skins, it would make a lovely gown </s>
<s> Today I am getting better ideas about distances </s>
<s> I was so eager to get hold of every pretty thing that I giddily grabbed for it, sometimes when it was too far off, and sometimes when it was but six inches away but seemed a foot--alas, with thorns between </s>
<s> I learned a lesson; also I made an axiom, all out of my own head--my very first one; THE SCRATCHED EXPERIMENT SHUNS THE THORN </s>
<s> I think it is a very good one for one so young </s>
<s> I followed the other Experiment around, yesterday afternoon, at a distance, to see what it might be for, if I could </s>
<s> But I was not able to make out </s>
<s> I think it is a man </s>
<s> I had never seen a man, but it looked like one, and I feel sure that that is what it is </s>
<s> I realize that I feel more curiosity about it than about any of the other reptiles </s>
<s> If it is a reptile, and I suppose it is; for it has frowzy hair and blue eyes, and looks like a reptile </s>
<s> It has no hips; it tapers like a carrot; when it stands, it spreads itself apart like a derrick; so I think it is a reptile, though it may be architecture </s>
<s> I was afraid of it at first, and started to run every time it turned around, for I thought it was going to chase me; but by and by I found it was only trying to get away, so after that I was not timid any more, but tracked it along, several hours, about twenty yards behind, which made it nervous and unhappy </s>
<s> At last it was a good deal worried, and climbed a tree </s>
<s> I waited a good while, then gave it up and went home </s>
<s> Today the same thing over </s>
<s> I've got it up the tree again </s>
<s> SUNDAY.--It is up there yet </s>
<s> Resting, apparently </s>
<s> But that is a subterfuge: Sunday isn't the day of rest; Saturday is appointed for that </s>
<s> It looks to me like a creature that is more interested in resting than it anything else </s>
<s> It would tire me to rest so much </s>
<s> It tires me just to sit around and watch the tree </s>
<s> I do wonder what it is for; I never see it do anything </s>
<s> They returned the moon last night, and I was SO happy </s>
<s> I think it is very honest of them </s>
<s> It slid down and fell off again, but I was not distressed; there is no need to worry when one has that kind of neighbors; they will fetch it back </s>
<s> I wish I could do something to show my appreciation </s>
<s> I would like to send them some stars, for we have more than we can use </s>
<s> I mean I, not we, for I can see that the reptile cares nothing for such things </s>
<s> It has low tastes, and is not kind </s>
<s> When I went there yesterday evening in the gloaming it had crept down and was trying to catch the little speckled fishes that play in the pool, and I had to clod it to make it go up the tree again and let them alone </s>
<s> I wonder if THAT is what it is for </s>
<s> Hasn't it any heart </s>
<s> Hasn't it any compassion for those little creature </s>
<s> Can it be that it was designed and manufactured for such ungentle work </s>
<s> It has the look of it </s>
<s> One of the clods took it back of the ear, and it used language </s>
<s> It gave me a thrill, for it was the first time I had ever heard speech, except my own </s>
<s> I did not understand the words, but they seemed expressive </s>
<s> When I found it could talk I felt a new interest in it, for I love to talk; I talk, all day, and in my sleep, too, and I am very interesting, but if I had another to talk to I could be twice as interesting, and would never stop, if desired </s>
<s> If this reptile is a man, it isn't an IT, is it </s>
<s> That wouldn't be grammatical, would it </s>
<s> I think it would be HE </s>
<s> I think so </s>
<s> In that case one would parse it thus: nominative, HE; dative, HIM; possessive, HIS'N </s>
<s> Well, I will consider it a man and call it he until it turns out to be something else </s>
<s> This will be handier than having so many uncertainties </s>
<s> NEXT WEEK SUNDAY.--All the week I tagged around after him and tried to get acquainted </s>
<s> I had to do the talking, because he was shy, but I didn't mind it </s>
<s> He seemed pleased to have me around, and I used the sociable "we" a good deal, because it seemed to flatter him to be included </s>
<s> WEDNESDAY.--We are getting along very well indeed, now, and getting better and better acquainted </s>
<s> He does not try to avoid me any more, which is a good sign, and shows that he likes to have me with him </s>
<s> That pleases me, and I study to be useful to him in every way I can, so as to increase his regard </s>
<s> During the last day or two I have taken all the work of naming things off his hands, and this has been a great relief to him, for he has no gift in that line, and is evidently very grateful </s>
<s> He can't think of a rational name to save him, but I do not let him see that I am aware of his defect </s>
<s> Whenever a new creature comes along I name it before he has time to expose himself by an awkward silence </s>
<s> In this way I have saved him many embarrassments </s>
<s> I have no defect like this </s>
<s> The minute I set eyes on an animal I know what it is </s>
<s> I don't have to reflect a moment; the right name comes out instantly, just as if it were an inspiration, as no doubt it is, for I am sure it wasn't in me half a minute before </s>
<s> I seem to know just by the shape of the creature and the way it acts what animal it is </s>
<s> When the dodo came along he thought it was a wildcat--I saw it in his eye </s>
<s> But I saved him </s>
<s> And I was careful not to do it in a way that could hurt his pride </s>
<s> I just spoke up in a quite natural way of pleasing surprise, and not as if I was dreaming of conveying information, and said, "Well, I do declare, if there isn't the dodo" </s>
<s> I explained--without seeming to be explaining--how I know it for a dodo, and although I thought maybe he was a little piqued that I knew the creature when he didn't, it was quite evident that he admired me </s>
<s> That was very agreeable, and I thought of it more than once with gratification before I slept </s>
<s> How little a thing can make us happy when we feel that we have earned it </s>
<s> THURSDAY.--my first sorrow </s>
<s> Yesterday he avoided me and seemed to wish I would not talk to him </s>
<s> I could not believe it, and thought there was some mistake, for I loved to be with him, and loved to hear him talk, and so how could it be that he could feel unkind toward me when I had not done anything </s>
<s> But at last it seemed true, so I went away and sat lonely in the place where I first saw him the morning that we were made and I did not know what he was and was indifferent about him; but now it was a mournful place, and every little think spoke of him, and my heart was very sore </s>
<s> I did not know why very clearly, for it was a new feeling; I had not experienced it before, and it was all a mystery, and I could not make it out </s>
<s> But when night came I could not bear the lonesomeness, and went to the new shelter which he has built, to ask him what I had done that was wrong and how I could mend it and get back his kindness again; but he put me out in the rain, and it was my first sorrow </s>
<s> SUNDAY.--It is pleasant again, now, and I am happy; but those were heavy days; I do not think of them when I can help it </s>
<s> I tried to get him some of those apples, but I cannot learn to throw straight </s>
<s> I failed, but I think the good intention pleased him </s>
<s> They are forbidden, and he says I shall come to harm; but so I come to harm through pleasing him, why shall I care for that harm </s>

<s> But he did not care for it </s>
<s> It is strange </s>
<s> If he should tell me his name, I would care </s>
<s> I think it would be pleasanter in my ears than any other sound </s>
<s> He talks very little </s>

<s> It is such a pity that he should feel so, for brightness is nothing; it is in the heart that the values lie </s>
<s> I wish I could make him understand that a loving good heart is riches, and riches enough, and that without it intellect is poverty </s>

<s> He evidently recognized, himself, that it was a good one, for he worked in in twice afterward, casually </s>
<s> It was good casual art, still it showed that he possesses a certain quality of perception </s>

<s> I do not think I have ever used it </s>

<s> ah, I shall never forget that--never, never </s>

<s> TUESDAY.--All the morning I was at work improving the estate; and I purposely kept away from him in the hope that he would get lonely and come </s>
<s> But he did not </s>
<s> At noon I stopped for the day and took my recreation by flitting all about with the bees and the butterflies and reveling in the flowers, those beautiful creatures that catch the smile of God out of the sky and preserve it </s>
<s> I gathered them, and made them into wreaths and garlands and clothed myself in them while I ate my luncheon--apples, of course; then I sat in the shade and wished and waited </s>

<s> Nothing would have come of it, for he does not care for flowers </s>
<s> He called them rubbish, and cannot tell one from another, and thinks it is superior to feel like that </s>

<s> A thin, transparent bluish film rose out of the hole, and I dropped everything and ran </s>

<s> and took it out again </s>
<s> It was a cruel pain </s>
<s> I put my finger in my mouth; and by standing first on one foot and then the other, and grunting, I presently eased my misery; then I was full of interest, and began to examine </s>
<s> I was curious to know what the pink dust was </s>

<s> It was FIRE </s>
<s> I was as certain of it as a person could be of anything in the world </s>
<s> So without hesitation I named it that--fire </s>
<s> I had created something that didn't exist before; I had added a new thing to the world's uncountable properties; I realized this, and was proud of my achievement, and was going to run and find him and tell him about it, thinking to raise myself in his esteem--but I reflected, and did not do it </s>

<s> He picked up one to examine it, but changed his mind and put it down again </s>
<s> Then he went away </s>
<s> NOTHING interests him </s>
<s> But I was interested </s>
<s> There were ashes, gray and soft and delicate and pretty--I knew what they were at once </s>
<s> And the embers; I knew the embers, too </s>
<s> I found my apples, and raked them out, and was glad; for I am very young and my appetite is active </s>
<s> But I was disappointed; they were all burst open and spoiled </s>
<s> Spoiled apparently; but it was not so; they were better than raw ones </s>
<s> Fire is beautiful; some day it will be useful, I think </s>
<s> FRIDAY.--I saw him again, for a moment, last Monday at nightfall, but only for a moment </s>
<s> I was hoping he would praise me for trying to improve the estate, for I had meant well and had worked hard </s>
<s> But he was not pleased, and turned away and left me </s>
<s> He was also displeased on another account: I tried once more to persuade him to stop going over the Falls </s>
<s> That was because the fire had revealed to me a new passion--quite new, and distinctly different from love, grief, and those others which I had already discovered--FEAR </s>
<s> And it is horrible!--I wish I had never discovered it; it gives me dark moments, it spoils my happiness, it makes me shiver and tremble and shudder </s>
<s> But I could not persuade him, for he has not discovered fear yet, and so he could not understand me </s>
<s> EXTRACT FROM ADAM'S DIARY Perhaps I ought to remember that she is very young, a mere girl and make allowances </s>
<s> She is all interest, eagerness, vivacity, the world is to her a charm, a wonder, a mystery, a joy; she can't speak for delight when she finds a new flower, she must pet it and caress it and smell it and talk to it, and pour out endearing names upon it </s>
<s> And she is color-mad: brown rocks, yellow sand, gray moss, green foliage, blue sky; the pearl of the dawn, the purple shadows on the mountains, the golden islands floating in crimson seas at sunset, the pallid moon sailing through the shredded cloud-rack, the star-jewels glittering in the wastes of space--none of them is of any practical value, so far as I can see, but because they have color and majesty, that is enough for her, and she loses her mind over them </s>
<s> If she could quiet down and keep still a couple minutes at a time, it would be a reposeful spectacle </s>
<s> In that case I think I could enjoy looking at her; indeed I am sure I could, for I am coming to realize that she is a quite remarkably comely creature--lithe, slender, trim, rounded, shapely, nimble, graceful; and once when she was standing marble-white and sun-drenched on a boulder, with her young head tilted back and her hand shading her eyes, watching the flight of a bird in the sky, I recognized that she was beautiful </s>
<s> MONDAY NOON.--If there is anything on the planet that she is not interested in it is not in my list </s>
<s> There are animals that I am indifferent to, but it is not so with her </s>
<s> She has no discrimination, she takes to all of them, she thinks they are all treasures, every new one is welcome </s>
<s> When the mighty brontosaurus came striding into camp, she regarded it as an acquisition, I considered it a calamity; that is a good sample of the lack of harmony that prevails in our views of things </s>
<s> She wanted to domesticate it, I wanted to make it a present of the homestead and move out </s>
<s> She believed it could be tamed by kind treatment and would be a good pet; I said a pet twenty-one feet high and eighty-four feet long would be no proper thing to have about the place, because, even with the best intentions and without meaning any harm, it could sit down on the house and mash it, for any one could see by the look of its eye that it was absent-minded </s>
<s> Still, her heart was set upon having that monster, and she couldn't give it up </s>
<s> She thought we could start a dairy with it, and wanted me to help milk it; but I wouldn't; it was too risky </s>
<s> The sex wasn't right, and we hadn't any ladder anyway </s>
<s> Then she wanted to ride it, and look at the scenery </s>
<s> Thirty or forty feet of its tail was lying on the ground, like a fallen tree, and she thought she could climb it, but she was mistaken; when she got to the steep place it was too slick and down she came, and would have hurt herself but for me </s>
<s> Was she satisfied now </s>
<s> No </s>
<s> Nothing ever satisfies her but demonstration; untested theories are not in her line, and she won't have them </s>
<s> It is the right spirit, I concede it; it attracts me; I feel the influence of it; if I were with her more I think I should take it up myself </s>
<s> Well, she had one theory remaining about this colossus: she thought that if we could tame it and make him friendly we could stand in the river and use him for a bridge </s>
<s> It turned out that he was already plenty tame enough--at least as far as she was concerned--so she tried her theory, but it failed: every time she got him properly placed in the river and went ashore to cross over him, he came out and followed her around like a pet mountain </s>
<s> Like the other animals </s>
<s> They all do that </s>
<s> FRIDAY.--Tuesday--Wednesday--Thursday--and today: all without seeing him </s>
<s> It is a long time to be alone; still, it is better to be alone than unwelcome </s>
<s> I HAD to have company--I was made for it, I think--so I made friends with the animals </s>
<s> They are just charming, and they have the kindest disposition and the politest ways; they never look sour, they never let you feel that you are intruding, they smile at you and wag their tail, if they've got one, and they are always ready for a romp or an excursion or anything you want to propose </s>
<s> I think they are perfect gentlemen </s>
<s> All these days we have had such good times, and it hasn't been lonesome for me, ever </s>
<s> Lonesome </s>
<s> No, I should say not </s>
<s> Why, there's always a swarm of them around--sometimes as much as four or five acres--you can't count them; and when you stand on a rock in the midst and look out over the furry expanse it is so mottled and splashed and gay with color and frisking sheen and sun-flash, and so rippled with stripes, that you might think it was a lake, only you know it isn't; and there's storms of sociable birds, and hurricanes of whirring wings; and when the sun strikes all that feathery commotion, you have a blazing up of all the colors you can think of, enough to put your eyes out </s>
<s> We have made long excursions, and I have seen a great deal of the world; almost all of it, I think; and so I am the first traveler, and the only one </s>
<s> When we are on the march, it is an imposing sight--there's nothing like it anywhere </s>
<s> For comfort I ride a tiger or a leopard, because it is soft and has a round back that fits me, and because they are such pretty animals; but for long distance or for scenery I ride the elephant </s>
<s> He hoists me up with his trunk, but I can get off myself; when we are ready to camp, he sits and I slide down the back way </s>
<s> The birds and animals are all friendly to each other, and there are no disputes about anything </s>
<s> They all talk, and they all talk to me, but it must be a foreign language, for I cannot make out a word they say; yet they often understand me when I talk back, particularly the dog and the elephant </s>
<s> It makes me ashamed </s>
<s> It shows that they are brighter than I am, for I want to be the principal Experiment myself--and I intend to be, too </s>
<s> I have learned a number of things, and am educated, now, but I wasn't at first </s>
<s> I was ignorant at first </s>
<s> At first it used to vex me because, with all my watching, I was never smart enough to be around when the water was running uphill; but now I do not mind it </s>
<s> I have experimented and experimented until now I know it never does run uphill, except in the dark </s>
<s> I know it does in the dark, because the pool never goes dry, which it would, of course, if the water didn't come back in the night </s>
<s> It is best to prove things by actual experiment; then you KNOW; whereas if you depend on guessing and supposing and conjecturing, you never get educated </s>
<s> Some things you CAN'T find out; but you will never know you can't by guessing and supposing: no, you have to be patient and go on experimenting until you find out that you can't find out </s>
<s> And it is delightful to have it that way, it makes the world so interesting </s>
<s> If there wasn't anything to find out, it would be dull </s>
<s> Even trying to find out and not finding out is just as interesting as trying to find out and finding out, and I don't know but more so </s>
<s> The secret of the water was a treasure until I GOT it; then the excitement all went away, and I recognized a sense of loss </s>
<s> By experiment I know that wood swims, and dry leaves, and feathers, and plenty of other things; therefore by all that cumulative evidence you know that a rock will swim; but you have to put up with simply knowing it, for there isn't any way to prove it--up to now </s>
<s> But I shall find a way--then THAT excitement will go </s>
<s> Such things make me sad; because by and by when I have found out everything there won't be any more excitements, and I do love excitements so </s>
<s> The other night I couldn't sleep for thinking about it </s>
<s> At first I couldn't make out what I was made for, but now I think it was to search out the secrets of this wonderful world and be happy and thank the Giver of it all for devising it </s>
<s> I think there are many things to learn yet--I hope so; and by economizing and not hurrying too fast I think they will last weeks and weeks </s>
<s> I hope so </s>
<s> When you cast up a feather it sails away on the air and goes out of sight; then you throw up a clod and it doesn't </s>
<s> It comes down, every time </s>
<s> I have tried it and tried it, and it is always so </s>
<s> I wonder why it is </s>
<s> Of course it DOESN'T come down, but why should it SEEM to </s>
<s> I suppose it is an optical illusion </s>
<s> I mean, one of them is </s>
<s> I don't know which one </s>
<s> It may be the feather, it may be the clod; I can't prove which it is, I can only demonstrate that one or the other is a fake, and let a person take his choice </s>
<s> By watching, I know that the stars are not going to last </s>
<s> I have seen some of the best ones melt and run down the sky </s>
<s> Since one can melt, they can all melt; since they can all melt, they can all melt the same night </s>
<s> That sorrow will come--I know it </s>
<s> I mean to sit up every night and look at them as long as I can keep awake; and I will impress those sparkling fields on my memory, so that by and by when they are taken away I can by my fancy restore those lovely myriads to the black sky and make them sparkle again, and double them by the blur of my tears </s>
<s> After the Fall When I look back, the Garden is a dream to me </s>
<s> It was beautiful, surpassingly beautiful, enchantingly beautiful; and now it is lost, and I shall not see it any more </s>
<s> The Garden is lost, but I have found HIM, and am content </s>
<s> He loves me as well as he can; I love him with all the strength of my passionate nature, and this, I think, is proper to my youth and sex </s>
<s> If I ask myself why I love him, I find I do not know, and do not really much care to know; so I suppose that this kind of love is not a product of reasoning and statistics, like one's love for other reptiles and animals </s>
<s> I think that this must be so </s>
<s> I love certain birds because of their song; but I do not love Adam on account of his singing--no, it is not that; the more he sings the more I do not get reconciled to it </s>
<s> Yet I ask him to sing, because I wish to learn to like everything he is interested in </s>
<s> I am sure I can learn, because at first I could not stand it, but now I can </s>
<s> It sours the milk, but it doesn't matter; I can get used to that kind of milk </s>
<s> It is not on account of his brightness that I love him--no, it is not that </s>
<s> He is not to blame for his brightness, such as it is, for he did not make it himself; he is as God make him, and that is sufficient </s>
<s> There was a wise purpose in it, THAT I know </s>
<s> In time it will develop, though I think it will not be sudden; and besides, there is no hurry; he is well enough just as he is </s>
<s> It is not on account of his gracious and considerate ways and his delicacy that I love him </s>
<s> No, he has lacks in this regard, but he is well enough just so, and is improving </s>
<s> It is not on account of his industry that I love him--no, it is not that </s>
<s> I think he has it in him, and I do not know why he conceals it from me </s>
<s> It is my only pain </s>
<s> Otherwise he is frank and open with me, now </s>
<s> I am sure he keeps nothing from me but this </s>
<s> It grieves me that he should have a secret from me, and sometimes it spoils my sleep, thinking of it, but I will put it out of my mind; it shall not trouble my happiness, which is otherwise full to overflowing </s>
<s> It is not on account of his education that I love him--no, it is not that </s>
<s> He is self-educated, and does really know a multitude of things, but they are not so </s>
<s> It is not on account of his chivalry that I love him--no, it is not that </s>
<s> He told on me, but I do not blame him; it is a peculiarity of sex, I think, and he did not make his sex </s>
<s> Of course I would not have told on him, I would have perished first; but that is a peculiarity of sex, too, and I do not take credit for it, for I did not make my sex </s>
<s> Then why is it that I love him </s>
<s> MERELY BECAUSE HE IS MASCULINE, I think </s>
<s> At bottom he is good, and I love him for that, but I could love him without it </s>
<s> If he should beat me and abuse me, I should go on loving him </s>
<s> I know it </s>
<s> It is a matter of sex, I think </s>
<s> He is strong and handsome, and I love him for that, and I admire him and am proud of him, but I could love him without those qualities </s>
<s> He he were plain, I should love him; if he were a wreck, I should love him; and I would work for him, and slave over him, and pray for him, and watch by his bedside until I died </s>
<s> Yes, I think I love him merely because he is MINE and is MASCULINE </s>
<s> There is no other reason, I suppose </s>
<s> And so I think it is as I first said: that this kind of love is not a product of reasonings and statistics </s>
<s> It just COMES--none knows whence--and cannot explain itself </s>
<s> And doesn't need to </s>
<s> It is what I think </s>
<s> But I am only a girl, the first that has examined this matter, and it may turn out that in my ignorance and inexperience I have not got it right </s>
<s> Forty Years Later It is my prayer, it is my longing, that we may pass from this life together--a longing which shall never perish from the earth, but shall have place in the heart of every wife that loves, until the end of time; and it shall be called by my name </s>
<s> But if one of us must go first, it is my prayer that it shall be I; for he is strong, I am weak, I am not so necessary to him as he is to me--life without him would not be life; now could I endure it </s>
<s> This prayer is also immortal, and will not cease from being offered up while my race continues </s>
<s> I am the first wife; and in the last wife I shall be repeated </s>
